Commentary

Research on Korean Immigration to the Northeast

(Part 3) Bin

Since the Sino-Japanese War in the 21st year of Guangxu's reign and the signing of the Treaty of Shimonoseki, Japan nominally forced us to recognize Korea as an independent country, but in reality, it took its place. From then on, Koreans, suffering from Japanese oppression, immigrated in increasing numbers. The Japanese further instigated animosity between the Chinese and Korean peoples in order to seize the four counties of Yanbian. The "Gando" dispute in the 33rd year of Guangxu's reign exposed Japan's initial ambition to invade the Northeast.

After the Russo-Japanese War, Japan's ambition to invade our Northeast became even more urgent. After many negotiations, in the first year of the reign of Emperor Xuantong of the Qing dynasty, it signed the Sino-Korean Border Affairs Treaty of the Tumen River and the Five Articles of Negotiation on the Three Eastern Provinces with Japan. In exchange for the reconstruction of the Anfeng Railway and the mining rights of the Fushun and Yantai coal mines, Japan finally recognized the four counties of Yanbian as our territory. The treaty recognized the land north of the Tumen River as a mixed residence area. The people of both China and Korea had to receive the same treatment there. With this convenience, even more Koreans migrated. Since Japan annexed Korea, the Japanese colonized Korean soldiers, and Koreans were forced to cross the Yalu and Tumen rivers to enter the Northeast. At that time, our border areas were being developed and needed people. As a result, the immigration of Koreans became as numerous as crucian carp crossing the river. Villages faced each other, scattered like stars in the sky. Since the founding of the Republic, under Japan's immigration policy, Koreans, backed by their political power and aided by semi-official organizations such as the Oriental Development Company and the South Manchuria Railway Company, increased their immigration to the Northeast year by year. According to Japanese surveys, the state of Korean migration in the corner of Yanbian is approximately as shown in the following table.

Korean Population

Year End of Year Population Annual Increase or Decrease Annual Increase or Decrease Rate

Republic of China Year 1 163,000

Year 5 203,961 (Plus) 40,426 0.199

Year 7 253,961 (Plus) 50,535 0.198

Year 8 279,150 (Plus) 25,189 0.090

Year 10 307,806 (Plus) 28,656 0.093

Year 11 33,806 (Plus) 16,000 0.042

Year 12 33,011 (Minus) 795 (Minus) 0.009

Year 13 329,591 (Plus) 6,580 0.019

Year 14 346,194 (Plus) 16,803 0.049

Year 15 356,016 (Plus) 9,822 0.028

Year 16 368,827 (Plus) 12,811 0.055

Year 17 582,950 (Plus) 14,103 0.038

Year 18 381,561 (Plus) 1,369 0.004

The above-mentioned history of Korean immigration in Yanbian is actually the beginning of Korean intrusion into our Northeast. It also spread from this central area of immigration to various places, creating a major problem in the heart of our Northeast today. This serious border issue has been delayed for decades without a solution. Is it any wonder that the Wanpaoshan incident occurred today?

(4) The Current Status of Korean Immigration to the Northeast

The history of Korean immigration to our Northeast has been roughly described above. After decades of accumulation, the fertile land and abundant resources of our Northeast have become like a second homeland for the "simply dressed" remnants of the Three Hans. The trend of Korean people migrating from various provinces in the heart of the Three Hans is increasing day by day. The speed of the increase in numbers is alarming. We allow others to sleep soundly beside our bed. They even overstep their bounds, turning from guests into hosts. The loss of sovereignty and the endless hidden dangers make us shudder.

To understand the current situation of Koreans in our Northeast, we must first examine where the most Koreans reside and how many there are. Our country has never paid attention to various statistics. To this day, there is still a lack of accurate statistics on the Chinese and foreign populations in various cities. It goes without saying that there is even less information on the Korean immigrants who come and go without a trace in the remote border areas of the Northeast. Although there have been surveys in the Northeast, they are inconsistent and make it difficult to choose. Japanese surveys often contain false records to confuse public opinion and are even more difficult to trust. Helplessly, let us compare the statistics from various sources to get a rough idea.

(1) According to a survey in Changchun at the end of 1929:

Liaoning Province: 455,125 people

Jilin Province: 556,320 people

Heilongjiang Province: 363,240 people

Total: 1,374,685 people (See "The Korean Issue in the Three Eastern Provinces" compiled by the Korean Provisional Government)

(2) According to a survey in Shenyang in early 1930:

Total for the three provinces: 1.3 million (See the same book)

(3) According to a survey by the Korean Compatriot Association of the Three Eastern Provinces in 1925:

Liaoning Province: 500,000 people, 10,000 naturalized

Jilin Province: 700,000 people, 100,000 naturalized

Heilongjiang Province: 100,000 people, 5,000 naturalized

Total: 1.3 million people, 115,000 naturalized

(4) According to a survey by the Eastern Railway Economic Bureau in 1929:

1. Residents in urban areas: 381,63 people

2. Residents in hinterland: 521,929 people

Total: 560,991 people

The above four statistics were all taken between 1929 and 1930. The smallest number is 560,091 people, and the largest number is 1,374,685 people. The difference is very large. Which one is reliable is difficult to determine. According to a report in the Shen Bao on February 2 of this year, "Since the ninth year of the Republic, the Japanese government has driven more than 3.7 million Korean people to immigrate to the Northeast in the name of colonization." This is an even greater difference from the above figures. In short, although none of the above figures can be considered accurate, the number of Korean immigrants in the Northeast today is at least between 1.3 million and 2 million. Such a huge amount of foreign immigration is unprecedented in the world. The significance of this matter for the future of our Northeast is self-evident to those with insight.

As for the distribution of Koreans in the Northeast, according to a survey by the Japanese Consulate, the following table shows:

Region Korean Population

Along the South Manchuria Railway 39,531

Liaoning 135,245

Jilin 54,661

Gando 382,390

Heilongjiang 7,449

(To be continued)

Important News

He Chengjun's Remarks

▲ Suppression of Communist Troops in Jiangxi Proceeding Smoothly

▲ Shi Yousan's Changes Inevitably Doomed to Failure

Hankou Correspondence: He Chengjun, Director of the Wuhan Provisional Headquarters, went to Gan this month on the 19th to visit Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek to seek instructions on matters such as the suppression of bandits and the administration of affairs. He stayed in Nanchang for two days. Commander-in-Chief Chiang gave detailed instructions on the secret matters of suppressing bandits on the borders of Hunan, Hubei, Sichuan, and the borders of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, as well as dealing with the situation in the North. Because of the importance of defense, it was inconvenient for him to stay for long. He took a special train from Nanchang to Xun on the morning of the 22nd, and then took the Taikoo Company's Poyang steamer westward. After receiving the telegram, the headquarters calculated that he would arrive in Hankou on the afternoon of the 23rd and notified the generals to gather at the riverbank to meet him. Those present included Xu Yuanquan, Director of Bandit Suppression and Rural Pacification in the Hunan, Hubei, and Sichuan border areas; Fan Shisheng, Commander of the 51st Division; Zhu Chuanjing, Chief of Staff of the Provisional Headquarters; Ye Peng, Chief of Staff of the Garrison Command; and brigade commanders Pan Shanzhai, Rong Jingfang, and Li Dingwu. At about 3:00 PM, the Poyang steamer arrived at the port. He got off the boat and went straight to the headquarters to take up his duties and meet with important people. He did not return to his private residence to rest until late in the evening. Xia Douyin, Commander of the Garrison, and Qian Dajun, Commander of the Fortress, who went with him, will arrive in Hankou a few days later because they are taking a detour to Mount Lu. After He returned to the headquarters, the reporter immediately visited him. According to him, the purpose of his trip to Gan was to report to Commander-in-Chief Chiang on the progress of bandit suppression and to seek instructions. The results were very satisfactory. The military situation in Gan Province is very smooth. Guangchang and Ningdu have been recovered one after another. The troops are taking advantage of the victory to pursue the bandits with great momentum. They are currently surrounding Donggu and will be able to capture it in a matter of days. After Donggu is recovered, the Red bandits will be wiped out in the near future. Commander-in-Chief Chiang will take advantage of the Red bandits' crushing defeat to visit Hankou this month. As for Shi Yousan's changes, rumors that he has been in contact with Commander Zhang's troops are not yet true. Shi's troops are not numerous, and abandoning obedience and following rebellion will inevitably lead to failure. Moreover, Han Fuqu, Sun Dianying, and the Jin-Sui generals are all sincerely supporting the Central Government and have sent telegrams denouncing Shi's absurdity. Commander Zhang is stationed in Beiping with full authority to handle the matter, which can be resolved smoothly. It is also heard that He has formed a committee to revise the business tax regulations in Hubei Province because the business tax has not improved after half a year of implementation. The committee has been officially established on the 24th. He will host a banquet for the chambers of commerce and industry associations at Yijiangchun on the same day to explain everything. (23rd)

Summary of Visits by Important Figures in Nanchang

▲ He, Xia, and Qian Stay for Two Days and Return to Hankou

▲ Yang and Ma's Representatives Arrive in Gan One After Another

▲ Yunnan Provincial Committee's Sichuan Representative Also Arrives

Nanchang Correspondence: After Chairman Chiang returned to Nanchang from the front line, many important figures came to Gan to pay their respects. He Chengjun, Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government and Director of the Wuhan Provisional Headquarters, arrived in Gan on the 20th with Qian Dajun and Xia Douyin, and stayed at the Jiangxi Grand Hotel. Immediately after unloading their luggage, they went to the headquarters to visit Chiang and report on the military and political affairs of Hubei Province, the suppression of bandits in the two lakes, and the joint suppression in various places on the borders of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Sichuan, Hubei, and Hunan, and to seek instructions. Chiang gave instructions on each matter. After He and the others took their leave, they went to the provincial government to meet Chairman Lu and discuss plans for suppressing bandits in Yangxin, Tongshan, Xiushui, Tonggu, and Pingliu, as well as the plans of Kong Hechong and Li Shixing. On the afternoon of the 21st, Lu hosted a banquet for He, Qian, and Xia at his private residence to discuss the issue of bandit suppression once again. This morning (22nd), He and the others went to the headquarters to bid farewell to Chiang, and then took a car from the headquarters to the crossing outside Zhang, and then transferred to the Niuhang Railway Station to take a train to Jiujiang, where they took a ship back to Hankou. On the same day, Hu Yimin, representative of Yang Hucheng, Chairman of the Shaanxi Provincial Government and Commander-in-Chief of the 17th Route Army, Tong Yaohua, representative of Ma Hongkui, Commander-in-Chief of the 15th Route Army, and Ma Wende, Deputy Commander of the 7th Army, arrived in the province by express train from Xun. After reporting to the headquarters, Chairman Chiang met with them separately and inquired about everything. Hu, Tong, and the others gave detailed reports on the military and political affairs of Shaanxi and the situation of the 15th Route Army in Lu, and conveyed everything on their behalf. Yesterday (21st), Sun Du and Zhang Weihan, members of the Yunnan Provincial Government, also arrived in Gan via the capital to report to Commander-in-Chief Chiang on the military and political situation in Yunnan Province and to seek instructions. Liu Xiang's representative arrived in the province a few days ago and reported on Sichuan's recent facilities and the situation of the various troops on behalf of Liu. He will return to Sichuan soon. (22nd)

Anti-Japanese Movement in Various Circles in Hunan Province

▲ Party, Government, Business, and Labor Circles Take Unified Action

▲ Economic Severance with Japan, Inspection of Enemy Goods

Changsha Correspondence: Since the Wanpaoshan incident occurred, people from all walks of life in Hunan Province have been extremely indignant. The recent anti-Japanese movement is described in detail as follows:

▲ Party and Government: The Provincial Party Affairs Steering Committee and the Provincial Government have successively issued circular telegrams, requesting all circles in the country to unanimously advocate serious negotiations on the Wanpaoshan case, promote domestic goods, and assist overseas Chinese. Japanese Consul-General to Hunan, Tani Renji, met with He Jian a few days ago to discuss official business. He spoke to the Japanese Consul about the indignation of Chinese people in various places, requesting that he inform the Japanese government to be aware of the situation and provide a satisfactory resolution to avoid the escalation of the turmoil. The Provincial Party Headquarters also telegraphed various counties and cities yesterday to hold mass rallies to assist the Wanpaoshan case and expand anti-Japanese propaganda.

▲ Business Circles: The business community is even more agitated about this case. The Changsha City Chamber of Commerce has telegraphed the banks in Shanghai and Hankou to stop handling Japanese goods. Meanwhile, the Provincial Federation of Commerce has issued a circular telegram, advocating that the government be urged to strictly instruct the diplomatic authorities to promptly lodge a serious protest and implement revolutionary diplomacy. It also stated that the Federation is determined to lead the businessmen of the province to implement economic severance and permanently boycott enemy goods as a support for the government. At a minimum, the Japanese side must apologize, compensate, and punish the murderers. At the same time, all unequal treaties between China and Japan must be abolished, and all outstanding cases from the past must be thoroughly resolved. If there is no satisfactory outcome, resolute measures should be taken, and the effort will not cease until the goal is achieved.

▲ Labor Circles: The Changsha City Trade Unions held an emergency meeting at the City Party Headquarters yesterday, the 21st, with representatives from various factories, totaling more than 2,000 people. They unanimously resolved to send a circular telegram to the country, striving for negotiations on the Wanpaoshan case, implementing economic severance with Japan, and permanently serving as a support for the government. They also requested the Central Government to seriously negotiate and vowed not to stop until the murderers were severely punished, losses were compensated, and the safety of overseas Chinese was permanently guaranteed.

▲ People's Congress: The Hunan people held a mass rally to assist the Wanpaoshan incident at the Provincial Education Association at 9:00 AM on the 22nd. All sectors of the Party, government, military, business, and academia participated. Workers from all factories stopped work for one day, assembled in teams to attend the meeting, and rickshaws stopped running for one day. All evening newspapers suspended publication for one day to express their indignation. At that time, 50,000 to 60,000 people attended the meeting, presided over by Tan Changkai, who explained the details of the tragic case and the attitude that the Chinese people should take. Finally, it was resolved to announce the crimes of the Japanese in a circular telegram, to request the Central Government to seriously negotiate, to request the people of the whole country to rise up together to resist foreign aggression, and to organize the "Hunan People's Support Association for Anti-Japanese Diplomacy." Fang Xiaochuan, Chen Jieshi, Xu Shu, Zhou Naixia, Liang Guodong, Wei Zhenbang, Tang Gan, Yu Fu, Tang Qiufan, Wang Shouren, Zhang Tiexiang, Chen Su, Liu Yunxiu, Feng He'an, Shi Chuncai, Liu Zhenpeng, Peng Jiaren, and Liu Wonan were elected as members, and the association was established on the same day to implement the inspection of enemy goods and economic severance with Japan, until 12:00 PM, when slogans were shouted and the meeting was adjourned. (July 22nd)

Continued News on Anti-Japanese Sentiment in Wuhan

Hankou Correspondence: All sectors of society in Hankou held an anti-Japanese and overseas Chinese protection conference on the 18th to assist overseas Chinese in resisting Japanese violence, telegraphed the Central Government to conduct serious negotiations, and resolved to organize an anti-Japanese association to implement economic severance with the Japanese. Responsible persons were designated to start preparations, and the preparatory committee appointed Wang Jinxia, Lu Shoupeng, Gao Bochang, and others to draft the outline of the organization to be formally established within a week. As for the boycott of Japanese goods, preparations are also underway. The City Chamber of Commerce has notified all industry associations to ban Japanese goods and donate money to help distressed overseas Chinese. The announcement is recorded as follows: "It has been found that in the Wanpaoshan village in Changchun County, Jilin Province, Korean farmers forcibly reclaimed paddy fields. The Japanese took the opportunity to implement a new attempt at their Manchuria-Mongolia policy. On the one hand, they occupied Wanpaoshan by force to protect Korean farmers and continue their illegal work. On the other hand, they incited Korean people to riot and massacre overseas Chinese. Alas, our overseas Chinese compatriots, countless have died, and thousands are fleeing back to the country every day. The situation is extremely embarrassing, with refugees everywhere. External disasters are compounding each other, and there is no basis for return. This is truly a cry to heaven that cannot be stopped. All colleagues in our industries, aware of this tragedy, must have the same compassion to provide relief. We hope that you will show great compassion and donate as much as possible to help the disaster-stricken overseas Chinese. Please also report the amount of funds raised at any time for statistical distribution. This case is of great importance. In addition to telegraphing to vow to support the government to the death, the association should immediately automatically sever economic ties with Japan. From now on, all businesses are strictly prohibited from ordering Japanese goods. We vow to persevere in our determination and avoid being ridiculed for half-heartedness. We hope that all our colleagues will be loyal and enthusiastic, and work together to save the situation. Then we will be very fortunate." (23rd)

▲ Helping Korean Overseas Chinese

More than 200 representatives attended. Lin Puxuan, a member of the county party headquarters, presided over the meeting. More Refugees Arrive in Andong

▲ Returning Because Homes Were Destroyed and Fortunes Were Lost, Making Survival Impossible

▲ More Than Six Hundred People Have Arrived in the Last Three Days

Andong Correspondence: The Andong General Chamber of Commerce received an urgent telegram from the Pyongyang Chinese Chamber of Commerce on the morning of the 18th, stating that Chinese people who had gone out to take refuge were returning one after another, and Chinese businesses in the city had all resumed operations and were trading as usual. However, there were about six or seven hundred unemployed Chinese people who had their homes burned down, their property completely lost, and were completely unemployed. They could not stay in Pyongyang, so they were sent back to the country to find another life to avoid starving to death in a foreign land. When these unemployed Chinese people enter the country, please take them in properly and provide them with some funds so that they do not become displaced. After receiving the telegram, the General Chamber of Commerce immediately notified the staff of the refugee reception center to prepare everything. That evening, the first batch of 320 unemployed Chinese people were sent from Pyongyang and sent to the Dangui Stage in the city for proper accommodation. In the past two days, the 19th and 20th, more than 200 people have arrived. According to the investigation by the staff of the refugee reception center, the number of people who have come to An from the Korean interior in recent days is as follows: 95 people on the 16th, 42 people on the 17th, 250 people on the 18th, and 64 people passed through Andong on the 19th and went directly to Changchun. Furthermore, since the 7th of this month, as of the most recent date, the total number of overseas Chinese from the Korean interior received by the reception centers in the city is 3,250, including 274 from Xuanchuan, 92 from Pyongyang, 44 from Dingzhou, 120 from Xin'anzhou.

Page 12

One person, 9 from Nanchuan, 39 from Pi County, 15 from Hanchuan, 10 from Hwanghae Province, 42 from Bukhadong, 4 from Baima River, 22 from Incheon, 85 from Bakcheon, and 18 from Tajima, and from Hainei. Those who have been sent to Shandong and upstream, Tonghua, Huanren, Ji'an, Linjiang, Kuandian, Changbai and other counties by the institute recently are free of charge by boat, and each person is given another two yuan of silver and ten buns. The cost of travel to North Korea is limited to Sinuiju, and those who go to the Northeast and North Manchuria to make a living will be given all the travel expenses regardless of the distance. The institute will purchase the tickets on its behalf, issue them temporarily at the station, and give another two yuan of silver before sending them to the train. Most of the incoming refugees have been dispersed, but the refugees from Pyongyang who have recently arrived are still being taken care of. (July 20th)

The Reality of Flooding in Hubei Province

▲ The Provincial Government Asks the Central Government and Other Provinces for Disaster Relief

Hankou Correspondence: Hubei Province is located on the Yangtze and Han rivers and has long been known as a land of lakes. Since the beginning of summer, excessive rainfall and dyke breaches have caused an unprecedented disaster. Continuous rain has not stopped for days, and the river water has risen sharply, almost level with the banks. Not only have fields and houses been submerged in the breaches, but Wuhan, which has always been known as a high-lying area, has also been obstructed due to waterlogging in the inner streets. The Zhanggong Dyke, which is the protection of Hankou, is often in danger of collapsing. People are panicked and cannot live in peace. The Hubei Provincial Government, aware that a major disaster has occurred and fearing that the dyke will collapse again and endanger Wuhan, has ordered the Water Conservancy Bureau to send personnel to investigate and take practical precautions, and the Garrison Department has sent teams to patrol to prevent reactionary bandits from taking the opportunity to sabotage. On the 23rd, it was submitted to the provincial government meeting for discussion. For the dykes along the Yangtze River in Wuhan, the Water Conservancy Bureau was ordered to take charge, and the Construction Department, the Water Police Bureau, the Hankou Municipal Government, and the Hankou Public Security Bureau were ordered to assist to ensure thoroughness. As for the most dangerous dykes in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, such as the Sandi Temple and Chewan dykes, and the Qianjiang and Jingshan dykes in the upper reaches of the Xiang River, the Water Conservancy Bureau has also sent personnel to survey and repair them at any time. If the rain stops within a few days, there may be no danger. In addition to the directors of the dyke works bureaus in the counties where the dykes have collapsed, who will be watched and punished separately, all disaster victims will first be provided with emergency relief using the rice stored in the Pingdiao. At the same time, the telegram requested the Central Relief Committee to allocate funds for disaster relief, saying, "Since the beginning of summer in Hubei Province, it has been raining for ten days, mountain floods have broken out, and the Yangtze and Han rivers have risen simultaneously, causing dyke breaches and submerging fields and houses. Even if the land is called high-lying and the fields belong to tombs, the upstream pours down, and the downstream tail is not open, which causes the drowning of wheat and the destruction of homes. The cries of sorrow of the living, and the dead buried in the bellies of fish. The tragedy of the disaster, and the magnitude of the disaster area, are rarely seen in recent times. In addition, years of banditry have resulted in a lack of hoarding of wealth, a lack of porridge for living, and no clean land to escape to. Hunger makes it difficult to leave the house, and life is imminent. Moreover, at a time of tension in the suppression of the Red Army, there is even more concern about the violence of a bad year. The tragic situation is unbearable to witness, and the crisis should be strictly prevented. In addition to sending personnel to various disaster areas to conduct detailed surveys, properly appease, and find ways to dredge and eliminate waterlogging, hoping to replant late rice, we are deeply afraid that the delay will be too long and the relief will be inadequate. We are specifically appealing to your association to consider the severity of the disaster in Hubei, to promptly allocate a large sum of money to purchase food and provide emergency relief in order to protect the lives of the people and spread kindness." At the same time, telegrams were sent to the provincial and municipal governments and local chambers of commerce, stating that we hope you will be compassionate and help your neighbors in need. We respectfully ask on behalf of all the disaster victims in Hubei. (July 23rd)

Regulations on Sichuan Province Post-War Rehabilitation Public Bonds

▲ Promulgated by the National Government Yesterday

▲ Fixed Amount of 20 Million Yuan

The Regulations on Sichuan Province Post-War Rehabilitation Public Bonds for the 20th Year of the Republic [1931] were promulgated by the National Government on the 25th. The original text is as follows: (Article 1) This public bond is named the Sichuan Province Post-War Rehabilitation Public Bond for the 20th Year of the Republic. (Article 2) The fixed amount of this public bond is 20 million yuan. (Article 3) The purpose of this public bond is specifically for post-war rehabilitation in Sichuan Province. (Article 4) The annual interest rate of this public bond is set at 8 percent, calculated from the date of issue, with interest paid on January 31st and July 31st each year. (Article 5) This public bond will be issued on August 1st of the 20th Year of the Republic [1931]. (Article 6) This public bond will be issued at 98 percent of its face value. (Article 7) Principal repayment of this public bond will occur every six months from the date of issue, with one-twentieth of the principal repaid each time, i.e., on January 31st and July 31st each year from January of the 21st Year of the Republic [1932] to July of the 30th Year of the Republic [1941]. Lottery drawings will be held 20 days before each repayment date. (Article 8) The Ministry of Finance will allocate 300,000 yuan monthly from the Central Government tax revenue within Sichuan Province, specifically from stamp, tobacco, and alcohol taxes, as a fund for principal repayment and interest payment. (Article 9) This public bond fund will be managed by a fund management committee. The repayment of principal and payment of interest will be handled by a bank designated by the fund management committee. A general association of the fund management committee will be established in Shanghai, composed of one representative each from the Ministry of Finance and the Auditing Department, one representative each from the Sichuan Post-War Rehabilitation Supervisor and the Sichuan Provincial Government, one representative from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, two representatives from the Shanghai Bankers' Association, one representative from the Shanghai Sichuan Business Community, and one representative from the Shanghai Sichuan Banking Industry. A branch association will be established in Chongqing, composed of one representative each from the Ministry of Finance and the Auditing Department, one representative each from the Sichuan Post-War Rehabilitation Supervisor and the Sichuan Provincial Government, one representative from the Chongqing Chamber of Commerce, and two representatives from the Chongqing Bankers' Association. The articles of association for the general association and branch association of the aforementioned fund management committee will be determined by the Ministry of Finance. (Article 10) This public bond will be in unregistered form. (Article 11) This public bond will be issued in four denominations: 10,000 yuan, 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, and 10 yuan. (Article 12) This public bond certificate may be freely mortgaged and traded, and may be used as a guarantee reserve for banks. If a security deposit is required for other official purposes, it may be used as collateral. (Article 13) Any act of counterfeiting this public bond or damaging its credit will be punished by the judicial authorities according to law. (Article 14) These regulations will take effect from the date of promulgation.

Continuous Torrential Rains Threaten Various Counties Along the Su-Yun Canal

▲ All Dams Returning to the Yangtze River Opened One After Another

▲ Opening the Dams Returning to the Sea Will Create a Waterlogged Country

▲ Public Opinion Divided into Factions For and Against Dam Opening

The upper reaches of the Grand Canal are fed by the Huai River. This summer, continuous rain has prevented the Huai River from discharging, causing the water level in the Grand Canal to rise continuously. The magnitude of the river's flow is unprecedented in decades. According to reports from the Water Conservancy Bureau yesterday, except for Gaoyou's Yu Matou, where the water level remains at 1.52 zhang, the water level has generally begun to drop due to the recent clear weather. Bengbu has dropped 5 centimeters but remains at 19.80 meters. Wan has dropped 2.3 centimeters but remains at 18.703 meters. Gouzha has risen 3 cun and remains at 1.9 zhang. These were affected by the Huai River surge of the past few days. In recent days, torrential rains have continued day and night, with over 2 chi of rainfall in the past two days and nights. Several sections of the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway have been flooded and impassable. In Zhenjiang, the river water has overflowed onto the riverbanks, turning the riverside roads into a watery land. Therefore, an increase in the water level of the Grand Canal is inevitable. Given this situation, it will be difficult to avoid opening the dams returning to the sea. However, considering the history of flood prevention along the Grand Canal, no matter what the water level, it is absolutely necessary to wait until a certain deadline after the autumn harvest to open the Cheluo, Xin Nanguan, and Sanba dams appropriately. As for the Zhongba dam, it has been abandoned, and the Zhaoguan dam has been closed for a long time due to its impact on the lives and property of hundreds of thousands of square miles. If the continuous rains do not stop, the downstream will also increase without decreasing. To protect the safety of the counties along the Grand Canal, it may be necessary to take action. It is reported that the provincial government has received urgent reports from various places these days. In addition to Director Sun personally departing to inspect the river, Hou Zhenping and Wang Jingtao were also dispatched yesterday to reside in Gaoyou and work on flood prevention. The farmers east and west of the river have different interests and are in conflict with each other. The people downstream are deeply afraid of the dam opening and are now gathered on the river embankment to try to prevent it. However, it is not yet known how the authorities will handle it.

Severe Flooding in Wuxi

▲ High and Low Fields Are All Submerged

▲ Grain Prices Are Gradually Increasing

Wuxi experienced heavy rain at the beginning of the month, causing river water to surge. The lowest fields were immediately submerged. On the 11th, there was a severe thunderstorm, and the water volume was higher than the first time. However, the lower fields could still be salvaged. Unexpectedly, starting on the 22nd, there was another continuous heavy rain, and the river water continued to rise by more than a chi. In the seventh district, Yangpo Dike and Huilong Dike, a total of more than 2,500 mu of fields, were mostly submerged. In the fifteenth district, the east and west Huajia Dikes, the upper, middle, and lower Sanyu, the north and south Xia Dikes, Tuotang Dike, the east and west Jiu Dikes, Liyang'an Dike, Dicheng Dike, Tianbao Gate Dike, and Loutan Dike were all submerged. Many small dikes collapsed. In the sixteenth district, Linzhuang Dike, etc., and in the fifth district, Hengpai Dike, were all submerged. Several dikes also collapsed. The low-lying fields along the lake have all been given up. In the lowest places, the water level is already level with the houses. Livestock have been washed away and lost. Transportation between the city and the countryside is completely cut off. The dikes in the four rural areas are in danger day and night. Farmers are working around the clock to reinforce the dikes. Although water pumps and wooden waterwheels are used to drain the water, there is no effect. Moreover, the dikes are only a few cun above the water surface, and the installation of axles is ineffective. If they want to build higher, there is no soil to be found. They can only let them collapse. As for the Furong Dike, which spans the three counties of Wuxi, Jiangyin, and Wujin, and the Yangjia Dike in the fifteenth and sixteenth districts, the inner dike is submerged in water like an upturned wok, and the outer dike is also in imminent danger. They are currently being defended. The city is a major grain distribution area, and all grain warehouses are located in the Beitang area. In recent days, the water has reached the shore and flooded the factory buildings. The warehouse owners are rushing to buy large quantities of pine planks to pile up the grain to prevent damage from water collapse. As a result, the price of pine planks has increased. Inch-thick planks are sold for 5.2 yuan per zhang. The rice market has also soared, from 10.6 yuan to 12 yuan. The situation in the flour market has also increased accordingly. The poor are constantly complaining. This year's wheat harvest was poor, and the silkworm industry failed. Farmers have little savings. Now, they have suffered from this flood. Since yesterday, farmers in various districts have reported famine and requested emergency relief. However, the disaster area is very large, and it may not be easy to investigate for the time being.

Local Communication

Changshu

A Strange Fire Occurs at Zhang Renji Confectionery. Zhang Renji Confectionery, Biscuit, and Foreign Wine Store, No. 58 Beishi Street, was opened by Zhang Junchang, a local resident, who also sold soda and other items. It has been in business for five years and the business has been fairly good. Unexpectedly, at approximately 10:00 AM on the 22nd, a fire suddenly broke out in the firewood room of the store for unknown reasons. Fortunately, it was discovered and extinguished with water. At that time, perhaps because there were still embers in the firewood pile, no attention was paid to it. Unexpectedly, at approximately 1:00 PM, smoke suddenly filled the area under the soda box under the stairs. It was quickly discovered by the staff and extinguished. Before long, the mosquito net upstairs suddenly caught fire. The people in the shop below were unaware of it. Soon, the flames burst out through the window, which was spotted by a rickshaw driver on the side of the road, who shouted, "Fire!" The neighbors were shocked and immediately rang the alarm bells everywhere. In no time, all the fire engines arrived and extinguished the fire. The dragon societies returned to their respective locations. Unexpectedly, the walls soon caught fire again, and then the bedding caught fire. No one could figure it out. The store owner and staff were busy fighting the fire. They closed the store doors and stopped doing business. The post office branch next door, recently established, was afraid of being affected by the fire that kept flaring up, so it moved all the important documents and mail to another location. The store owner was almost mentally deranged because he couldn't figure out the cause of the fire. He asked passersby, who said it was caused by fox spirits. Zhang went to various places to burn incense and make vows and invited Taoist priests to perform rituals at home. Unexpectedly, while the bells and drums were ringing and the Taoist priests were chanting, the calendar hanging on the wall suddenly caught fire. It is estimated that there were as many as eleven fires in half a day, which is truly unheard of. Fortunately, none of them spread. However, the neighboring residents were afraid that another disaster would occur at night, so they warned each other not to sleep.

The Old Case of Former County Magistrate Zhuang Yan's Embezzlement Is Brought Up Again. Zhuang Yeguang, the current director of the Finance Bureau of this county, is the son of Zhuang Yan, who served as the county magistrate of this county twice and also served as the county magistrate of Nantong. Last year, he was sentenced to three months in prison in Suzhou for visiting a prisoner, Lu Yuren, in Nantong and carrying and sending opium. When Zhuang was the county magistrate in this county, he was suspected of embezzling 4,000 yuan of public funds. It has now been discovered by citizen Chen Yingchun. It is recorded on the transfer of authority that Sun Chuanfang took away 4,000 yuan in military funds. He presented it vaguely for verification and cancellation. Now that his son Yeguang has come to Changshu as the head of finance, Chen once wrote to Yeguang, asking him to pay it on behalf of his father, with a deadline of ten days to reply. However, Zhuang did not reply. Now Chen has evidence that the former county magistrate Zhuang embezzled public funds and has drafted a complaint to the Supervisory Yuan, the Finance Department, and the chief prosecutor of the High Court, listing the evidence and formally accusing him, in the hope that the truth will come out. Chen Yingchun, courtesy name Housheng, was also a county government official when Zhuang was the county magistrate.

Wuxi

Change of Finance Bureau Chief. Shen Ruji, the chief of the Finance Bureau of Wuxi County, resigned due to financial exhaustion and difficulty in coping. The Director of Finance Department approved the resignation and transferred Gong Li, the chief of the Finance Bureau of Shanghai County, to Wuxi to take over. Chief Wang has arrived in Wuxi from Shanghai yesterday and decided to hand over today (26th). It is also heard that Chief Wang has decided to transfer Zhang Pengfei, the chief of the First Section. He arrived in Wuxi yesterday. Lu Dingxin, the chief of the Second Section, is still in Shanghai to handle the handover. The other staff members have also changed slightly.

Organizing the All-Circles Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee. All circles of agriculture, industry, commerce, and education in Wuxi gathered at the county party headquarters yesterday to discuss the issues of Korean people, instigated by the Japanese, massacring overseas Chinese in Korea and the countermeasures against Japan. Chairman Gui Wuchen resolved (1) to organize the All-Circles Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee, (2) to be organized by agriculture, industry, commerce, education, and legal organizations, (3) to hold the first meeting on the 27th of this month, (4) to request the central government to dismiss Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting, Ambassador to Japan Wang Rongbao, and Consul-General to Korea Zhang Weicheng, (5) to request the central government to clearly define foreign policy to show to the whole country.

Township Chiefs in the Seventeenth District Resign En Masse. Hua Sigu, the district chief of the seventeenth district (Fuan Township), is a graduate of the second session of the Jiangsu Province District Chief Training Institute. He initially served in the tenth district, where someone accused him of embezzlement, etc. Although he is now in his current position, the public sentiment is still mostly dissatisfied. A few days ago, all 25 township chiefs in the district submitted a petition to the county government, stating that Hua was selfish and derelict in his duties and that they were ashamed to work with him. They jointly requested to resign en masse. Yesterday, the county government instructed the township chiefs to order several representatives to be recommended to the case on the 29th to confront the district chief and then re-verify it.

Strange News of a Rural Woman Giving Birth to a Snake. Wang, the wife of Zhou Huanzhang, a villager in Linzhuang Village, near Linzhuang Bridge, Qingcheng Township, the fifteenth district of the county, became pregnant two years ago and has not yet given birth. Her abdomen is large and bulging, like a five-stone melon. The Huanzhang couple were very surprised. The day before yesterday, Wang felt a faint pain in her abdomen. Her husband knew that she was about to give birth and immediately hired a midwife to deliver the baby. After a while, Wang's abdominal pain increased, and suddenly she gave birth to a section of a snake's head, about five or six cun long, with a ferocious and terrifying appearance. However, the lower half of the snake did not come out for a long time. When the midwife saw this, she planned to put her hand in and take the snake out. Unexpectedly, the snake suddenly retracted completely. At that time, the news spread throughout the neighborhood, and those who went to watch filled the doorway, and everyone's faces changed. However, the pregnant woman Wang was still safe and sound. Her husband, Huanzhang, took his wife by boat to the city yesterday and admitted her to Puren Hospital. The hospital doctor performed surgery to remove the snake. Upon inspection, the snake was dead. Let it be noted for the research of physiologists.

A Quarrel Between Husband and Wife Turns Into a Tragedy. Chen Xuegan, the son of Chen Wenhao, a resident of No. 12 Taiding Bridge in the city, is 28 years old. He used to work at the Minxin Printing Company in Hongkou, Shanghai. Recently, Chen Xuegan returned to Wuxi because he was suffering from athlete's foot. The other night, Chen planned to spend time with his wife, Cheng. Cheng did not agree, which led to an argument. Chen Xuegan, in a moment of anger, took a sharp knife and stabbed Cheng's throat, causing her to bleed profusely and fall to the ground unconscious. Xuegan, knowing that he had caused a disaster, immediately abandoned the knife and fled. Later, someone reported it to the police, who immediately took the injured person to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau and transferred her to the Labor Hospital for treatment. At the same time, Chen Wenhao, Xuegan's father, was summoned to the bureau for questioning and ordered to post bail and wait for his son Xuegan to be arrested before further investigation.

Zhenjiang

The Liyang Bribery Case Raises Questions of Jurisdiction. In the case of former Liyang County Magistrate Li Jinfang reporting that former Finance Bureau Chief Pan Keping colluded with the county chamber of commerce members to commit bribery, the provincial government transferred the case file to the court for investigation and resolution. It is now heard that Li Jinfang has filed a further lawsuit against Pan Keping for bribery with the Zhenjiang Local Court. The prosecutor's office believed that Pan had worked at the National Revolutionary Army's 18th Division's Beijing Office and presented a letter of appointment from that office, causing doubts about jurisdiction. Yesterday, they submitted a request to the Jiangsu Higher Court Prosecutor's Office for verification and instructions and notified Li Jinfang. Continuous Heavy Rains Cause Tragedy. Since the heavy rain on the 2nd of this month, the Zhenjiang area has experienced many days of continuous rain, which has only slightly cleared up. Unexpectedly, in the past two days, there has been heavy rain again, especially at night. All the back alleys of the streets are flooded with water to the ankles, forming a vast expanse of water, almost like a swamp. The collapse of walls and houses is even more common. Yesterday morning, a portion of the Jingji Linghou Mountain collapsed due to the daily heavy rain erosion, causing the residents at the foot of the mountain, along with their houses, to be buried in the soil. After many people dug and picked, it was heard that two people were suffocated to death and two were injured, who were then taken to the hospital for treatment.

Huzhou

Mountain Floods Erupt, Steamships and Automobiles Completely Suspended. In the Huzhou area, there has been continuous heavy rain for the past half month, resulting in mountain floods and surging river waters. The lowest embankment is less than a chi from the river water. Therefore, all shipping companies are afraid of the impact on the embankment and the damage to farmland. On the 22nd, all steamships on the Shanghai-Huzhou, Hangzhou-Huzhou, Suzhou-Huzhou, and Southwest Township routes were completely suspended. However, the Shanghai-Huzhou route was able to operate as usual because it runs on Tai Lake. Also, the automobile road on the Hangzhou-Huzhou section was washed away in several places by mountain floods, and vehicles could not travel. All were temporarily suspended, resulting in the complete disruption of transportation in the Huzhou area. It is heard that yesterday, the 22nd, the Zhaoshang Lixing ships from Shanghai to Huzhou were stopped by the farmers in Pingwang this morning and were unable to move forward. The ships were temporarily docked in Pingwang and immediately telegraphed the two bureaus in this city. It is heard that the two shipping companies, after receiving the news, planned to hire many ferries tomorrow to go to the area to pick up and transport goods to Huzhou.

Director Chen of the Public Security Bureau Transferred to Jiashan. Chen Hongji, the director of the Public Security Bureau of Wuxing County in this city, has been in office for almost a year. Recently, someone falsely used the name of gentleman Li Huibo, etc., and accused him to the provincial government. Although Li Guangyu, the county magistrate of Wuxing County, investigated the truth and Li Huibo, etc., denied the accusations, Director Chen became passive because of this and repeatedly submitted his resignation to the Civil Affairs Department. The Civil Affairs Department has now approved Chen's transfer to be the director of the Public Security Bureau of Jiashan County.

Hangzhou

The Main Culprit in the Xu Zhuoran Assassination Case Will Be Escorted to Hangzhou. After the Xu Zhuoran assassination case in Fujian was transferred to the jurisdiction of the Hangzhou County Local Court last year, it was tried many times. On June 5th, it was announced that Chen Delin, Chen Yanxiang, Ye Caizhen, etc., were all innocent, and Lin Luo was sentenced to four years in prison. The prosecutor who investigated the case was dissatisfied and filed a public prosecution with the High Court, which was scheduled to open on August 11th. Yesterday, the High Court received a telegram from Mrs. Xu from Xiamen, which stated that the troops stationed in Tong'an, together with the county government, had arrested the bandit Lin Min, who was the murderer who assassinated Xu Zhuoran in this case, the person who was said to have died in the judgment of the Hangzhou County Local Court. In addition to telegramming the National Government, she requested that personnel be quickly dispatched to escort him to Hangzhou for trial so that justice could be served as soon as possible. It is heard that the High Court, after receiving the telegram, planned to send personnel to meet him and escort him to Hangzhou for trial on the opening date.

The Qingxiang Bureau Arrests a Large Number of Kidnappers. The Qingxiang Bureau of Hangzhou County recently learned that a large number of kidnappers were hiding near Pingyao, kidnapping people for ransom. It immediately dispatched many police officers, quietly, and rushed to arrest Li Zhongbang, Zhang Xunan, Luo Jinghua, Hu Liangfa, Xiao Shizhou, Zhang Jin, and the monk of a certain temple, Senlin, etc., nine people, and women Li Li, Yu Sun, and Xiang Chen, etc., four people, totaling thirteen people. It also seized a machete and many other stolen goods and sent them to the Hangzhou Local Court for detention and trial.

The Civil Affairs Department Strictly Handles the Drug Case on Qingnian Road. The Civil Affairs Department of Zhejiang, together with the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital, recently cracked a case of trafficking in a large number of drugs at No. 22 Qingnian Road, the Hangzhou Branch of the Huachang Paint Factory. All the drugs were ordered by the Public Security Bureau to be kept in custody. Later, several places were cracked in Tongxiang, Huangyan, Linhai, etc., and they were also tested by the Provincial Health Testing Institute, which confirmed that they were the same opium substitutes. This time, the Qingnian Road case is a branch office. The correspondence and distribution numbers show that it sells about a thousand yuan per month, divided into six grades: You, Te, Tian, Di, Ren, and Dan. The Civil Affairs Department is paying close attention to this case, and it is being transferred to the court or handled in another case. It is being submitted to the provincial government for approval and disposal.

Xiaoshan

Kidnappers Arrested and Hostage Rescued. Zhou Rujie, the director of the Linpu Public Security Branch Bureau in Shaoxing, heard that there was a bandit den in Shimenwang, the border between Shaoxing and Zhuji. He specially dispatched 20 policemen to search and arrest them. On the 23rd, he captured three bandits, Wang Amao, etc., and a seven-year-old hostage (the young owner of a Nanhuo store in Fuyang). In addition to reporting the case to the county government, the bandits have now been sent to the county for strict handling. Yesterday, the seven-year-old hostage was sent back to his original residence in Fuyang.

Eight Fish Thieves Sentenced to One Year and Six Months in Prison. Jiang Axi, Jiang Jin, Cao Xizhao, Cao Songshou, etc., eight notorious fish thieves in Shicuncao outside the South Gate of Xiaoshan, repeatedly stole fish from the Chen family and injured the fish managers Chen Bajin and Cai Xiangrong. The Chen family filed a complaint with the County Court. On the 24th, Fu Tingrui, the criminal judge, pronounced the verdict. As a result, the thieves, Cao Songshou, etc., eight people, were each sentenced to one year and six months in prison.

Shaoxing

The County Chamber of Commerce Asks for Instructions on How to Set Up Branch Offices. The Shaoxing County Chamber of Commerce, because the townships far from the city are requesting the establishment of branch offices to facilitate commercial affairs, telegraphed the Ministry of Industry on the 23rd, stating that Article 8 of the Chamber of Commerce Law clearly stipulates that the affairs of establishing branch offices shall be carried out by the employees of the chamber of commerce who reside or operate in the area of the branch office. Now, all the employees of this association are engaged in commerce in the city, and their residences are not in the area where the branch office is requested to be established. How should it be handled? It is reasonable to telegraph for verification and instructions.

Deadline for Ending Cases Reported by Villages and Li. The Shaoxing County Government, because the villages and li have not yet completed all the procedures for handling land reporting cases, because the method of surveying and measuring by year has been issued by the province, the cases reported cannot be concluded without sending police to supervise. Yesterday, a special order was issued to the Public Security Branch Bureaus to quickly send police to strictly pursue the unpaid map booklets, forms, and outstanding expenses and reporting procedures fees for the villages and li under their jurisdiction, in accordance with the separate items, and to collect them all by July 30th.

Municipal Education Issues a Circular Forbidding Teachers and Staff From Arbitrarily Holding Concurrent Positions

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to the principals of municipal secondary schools, stating that, as a principle, teachers and staff of municipal secondary schools should be full-time. Those who hold concurrent positions should comply with the regulations on restricting concurrent positions for teachers and staff of municipal secondary schools promulgated by the bureau. It has been found that there are still those who have not complied with the previous regulations in the second semester of the nineteenth year. This is truly inappropriate. At the beginning of this new school year, it is necessary to reiterate the previous order that teachers and staff of municipal secondary schools in the twentieth year shall not arbitrarily hold concurrent positions. Let all know and inform all teachers and staff. This order.

Xu Shiying Hosts Banquet for Anhui Fellow Provincials

▲For Raising Funds for Anhui Workers' Children's School

Xu Shiying, a respected figure from Anhui residing in Shanghai, hosted a banquet at Yipinxiang Restaurant for fellow Anhui provincials to discuss fundraising for the Anhui Workers' Children's School, which has been established for half a year but lacks funding and faces an uncertain future. During the banquet, Mr. Xu first reported on the school's purpose, followed by representatives such as Hong Junjiu, who reported on the school's establishment process. Then, Principal Pan Shanzhai delivered a speech, expressing his willingness to follow in the footsteps of his fellow elders to maintain the school's development and pledging 300 yuan. Subsequently, Guan Yunong, Hu Xiangjun, Wu Zhiping, and others pledged amounts ranging from 100 to 200 yuan. Mr. Xu then delivered a speech thanking his fellow provincials for their enthusiastic support, and stated that donations should be directly handed over to Mr. Hong Zhenjiu, the fund custodian of the school board. For those fellow provincials who did not attend, Mr. Xu also sent out letters soliciting donations. The letter respectfully stated that the Anhui Workers' Children's School in Shanghai was founded by fellow provincials residing in Shanghai, and has been open for half a year with commendable results. However, the school is in its early stages and lacks funding, which has caused difficulties in its operations. Furthermore, the current semester is about to end, and the next semester involves significant expansion, various equipment, and an urgent need for funds. Xu Shiying, as a fellow provincial, hosted a banquet at Yipinxiang Restaurant to invite fellow elders to discuss fundraising methods. However, due to limited effort, some invitation letters were inevitably missed, which is regrettable. Fortunately, all those who attended that day valued the children of workers, generously donated, and are deeply appreciated. It is believed that this matter is significant and relies on collective efforts. Now, Hong Junjiu, the school board's custodian, has sent someone forward, hoping for understanding and generous donations. This is not only fortunate for Xu Shiying and others. Respectfully wishing you well, Xu Shiying. It is now heard that more than half of the over 1,000 yuan pledged at the time has been received, so the equipment costs and the outstanding carpenter's fees and teacher salaries that Mr. Hong had advanced can all be paid in full. For those who did not attend, such as Mr. Sun Jingxi, have already voluntarily pledged 100 yuan, and said that if the fund reaches 10,000 yuan, the bank will be asked to provide voluntary assistance and earn 1,000 yuan in interest each year. Mr. Hong has discussed this with Mr. Xu. The decision on whether to deposit the received donations in Zhongfu Bank or Minxin Bank will be made after consulting with Mr. Sun Jingxi and Mr. Chen Zhengyou.

Chinese Basketball Shows Its True Colors, Sweeping Shanghai Business University in Shanghai

丨Forty-three to Thirteen丨

Shanghai Basketball Emerges as a Rising Force

Business University Suffers Five Losses and Two Wins in Seven Games

Last night, the Shanghai High School Affiliated to the University of Shanghai basketball team defeated the Japanese Tokyo University of Commerce team with a score of 43 to 13 in the China Basketball Hall. Shanghai High School dominated for a time, invincible, and the spectators sighed in admiration. The praise filled the ears. This was the last battle for the Business University team in Shanghai, but unexpectedly, they suffered such a blow. The Business University team is scheduled to return east on the 28th.

Shanghai High School Wins Big and Triumphantly

Last night's battle was enjoyable and cathartic. The momentum of the University of Shanghai was like a river flowing thousands of miles. After Feng Nianci broke through the basket, the generals scored one after another, two after two, until they reached eleven points. Business University was still at zero. At the end of the first half, Shanghai High School won big and triumphantly with a score of 17 to 4.

▲ Business University Was Dumbfounded

Business University was no match. Starting from the second half, Shanghai High School strung together a series of baskets, one after another, creating a new record of 33 to 6. Business University was dejected and dumbfounded, helpless, with its teachers turning their backs on the city. The entries and exits were hectic, but the defense could not keep up, let alone the offense. They were at a loss. Shanghai High School originally had the determination not to let them score more than ten points, but Lu Zhonghui left due to a leg injury. In the last five minutes, the Shanghai High School reserve team played, ending the game with a score of 43 to 13.

▲ The Majesty Before the Southern Expedition

Shanghai High School will change its name to Yangshupu Team and depart for the Southern Expedition on the 29th, as reported earlier. This battle can be said to be a trial run before the Southern Expedition. It was indeed extremely sharp, cutting iron like mud. It is a dynamic force in the West China YMCA this winter. The whole team is far from what it used to be. During the attack, the three routes advanced simultaneously, attacking from the left and right. Business University lost sight of one thing while focusing on another. The speed of the army was swift and elusive. The passing was smooth, neither detached nor sticky. Long shots and close shots were effortless. Business University had no chance to get the ball. The initial five-person defense was like a facade. The subsequent zone defense was easily broken through by Shanghai High School, and they were exhausted from running. They never imagined that Shanghai High School basketball would be so dominant.

▲ Overview of the Business University Team

The Business University team came to Shanghai and played a total of seven games, with five losses and two wins. To summarize, physical strength is their characteristic, and agility is also commendable. They did not lose their bravery in battle, but there is still a long way to go in terms of coordination and shooting accuracy. Yongi and Jinzi are two strong players in the team. However, the Japanese are willing to work hard, so they should not be underestimated. We should also strive for progress every day. The results of the seven games are as follows:

丨Referee: Lu Zhongen丨

Triangular Swimming Competition, the United States Takes the Lead

丨Total Score of Forty-three Points丨

Japan Second... Thirty-seven Points

China Third... Seventeen Points

▲Chris Breaks Shanghai Record in 100-Yard Breaststroke

The China-Japan-US triangular swimming competition was held at the YMCA swimming pool at 8 PM last night. Within two hours, the three countries competed against each other. As a result, the United States team won the championship with 43 points, Japan was second with 37 points, and China was third with 14 points. At the end of the battle, Fei Wusheng, the general secretary of the YMCA, presented the awards.

▲ The Nature of the Competition

This triangular competition was based on sports organizations. The Chinese team was temporarily organized by the Chinese Swimming Research Association, Japan was represented by the Japan Sports Association, and the United States was limited to YMCA members. It was called the China-Japan-US swimming competition, but in reality, it was just three groups in Shanghai, Japan, and the United States. Therefore, many good players from the three countries did not participate because they were limited by qualifications. Next year, the China National Sports Association plans to hold a grand international swimming competition, but there is no suitable swimming pool, so we can only wait until next year.

▲ One New Record

Among the nine events, except for the diving event, the 100-yard breaststroke performance was the best. Chris from the United States broke the record of 78 seconds set by Auster from the YMCA pool on November 12, 1929, with 77 seconds, creating a new Shanghai record. The 100-yard freestyle, the 100-yard medley, and the 100-yard backstroke were relatively good.

▲ China's Downturn

Not many of the Chinese team's players were skilled, and those who were proficient in the art stood by and watched. Therefore, in each competition, they fell behind step by step. Among the players, Yu Binqi, Yin Yanjun, and Tang Tianya were the most agile. Yu's start was unfavorable, and he was injured on the field, otherwise, it might have been more exciting.

▲ The United States Makes Great Efforts

In the first three events, the United States did not gain an advantage. They got eight points in the diving event and took the lead. It was not until the seventh event, the 200-yard medley, that no one entered the water. Before the third person's finger touched the edge of the pool, they were penalized and their position and points were canceled. As a result, the score ratio between the United States and Japan became 33 to 30, which was very close. The United States worked hard in the last two acts, hoping to take the lead. In the eighth act, Chris from the United States made a miraculous contribution, creating a new record. At that time, the United States took the lead by three points. The victory of the United States in the last event was already in their grasp, but they still won the championship with a fighting spirit, scoring 43 points.

▲ Japan Did Not Get Its Wish

Most of the events were Japan's strengths, so they had ambitions at the beginning of the competition. Sakakura, who attended the World Games, was also among them. In event after event, Japan competed with the United States for the lead, and repeatedly surpassed them. However, they suffered fatal injuries in the diving event and the 880-yard freestyle event, and ultimately fell behind the United States with 37 points, and retreated without getting their wish.

The Davis Cup Final Is Unprecedented, England and France Are Evenly Matched

丨Each Wins a Singles Group丨

丨15,500 Spectators丨

Paris, 24th - The weather is sunny and clear. The England-France Davis Cup Championship Final, the first day today, held at Roland Garros. The result is that the autumn colors are evenly divided, and each wins a singles group.

▲ Unprecedented Spectacle, 15,000 Spectators

Long before the start of the game, the stadium was already full. There were about 15,000 spectators, and there were thousands and thousands more outside the door who could not get in. The police tried their best to maintain order. The trees outside the venue were full of people, and the police could do nothing but let them do what they wanted. The grand occasion was unprecedented in history.

▲ Thrilling, the Shouts Were Thunderous

Because the strength of the two teams is evenly matched, and the fierce pre-war publicity, the victory and defeat of this game is unprecedented in tension. People from both sides cheered wildly, and the shouts shook the sky and the earth. Austin was thus frightened and defeated by Cochet. White kept calm, and Borotra was defeated.

▲ Results of the First and Second Singles

White (England) (4-6, 10-8, 6-0, 4-6, 6-4)

(Borotra (France))

Cochet (France) (3-6, 11-9, 6-2, 6-4)

Austin (England)

▲ White Wins Against Borotra

In the White-Borotra match, White had an excellent performance in the first set, but Borotra won 6-4. In the 18th game of the second set, Borotra's energy was exhausted and he lost. As a result, he was completely defeated in the third set, losing six games in a row. The fourth set was fiercely contested, and White won the last set with extremely accurate shots.

▲ Cochet Has Recovered His Original State

In the Cochet-Austin battle, Cochet had completely recovered to his original state before the typhoid fever. After failing in the first set, he often advanced to the front net to launch his artillery fire. In the 20th game, Cochet won 11-9. Austin was very good in the first set, and had a total of seven leads in the second set, but failed in the end. Unfortunately, he lost all his strength in the last two sets.

▲ The Victory or Defeat Depends on the Last Three Groups

Saturday is the doubles, and Sunday is the last two singles groups. Each won a singles group on the first day. England still insists that it is possible to win the cup. Considering the actual strength, it is not easy for France to win. The grand occasion of the spectators arises from this suspicion. However, France is more likely to win the doubles and the singles match between Cochet and White.

The match originally scheduled for the 26th of this month will be postponed to August 29 (Saturday).

Local News

Rain Affects Transportation

▲ Jinghu Train Interrupted

Due to continuous heavy rain and flash floods between the Zhenjiang South Gate Station and Zhenjiang Station on the Jinghu Railway, the Baogai Mountain tunnel collapsed, and mountain soil was washed down, causing blockage. At the same time, the tracks at Hepingmen and other places were also washed away, causing trains to be stranded. This situation was reported yesterday. Here is a continuation of yesterday's situation:

▲ Disaster Situation The disaster area is vast. Almost no place from Xiashu Station is unaffected by the flood. The most severely affected area is Gaozi Station, where the water level is about six feet above the ground, making it impossible for station personnel to reside. They are now being relocated to 40-ton covered wagons. Xiashu, Longtan, Hepingmen, and other places are flooded to a depth of about three to four feet. Many sections of track between Yaohuamen, Taipingmen, and Qixia Mountain were washed away. The houses of nearby residents were also washed away and disappeared without a trace. The collapse of the Baogai Mountain tunnel between Zhenjiang and Zhenjiang South Gate Station was due to loose mountain soil being washed down, causing blockage. At the same time, soil from the hills on both sides of the track also flowed down with the water, completely burying the tunnel. The collapsed soil is estimated to be about 250 cubic meters. The engineering department is now working on opening ditches to drain the water. If there is no heavy rain and the water recedes slightly, the passage can be directly opened for traffic within one or two days.

▲ Rescue Process After receiving the news the day before yesterday afternoon, the railway bureau immediately instructed the chief engineer of the engineering department to go to inspect the disaster situation overnight. Chen Zhongying, the chief of the traffic section, also went along. Immediately, small workers from the entire railway were called to concentrate at Zhenjiang South Gate Station to await orders. The Zhenjiang section engineer also personally rode a handcar in the rain yesterday morning to investigate the stations to facilitate phased construction. On the Nanjing side, the engineer stationed in Nanjing also led small workers from Nanjing Station yesterday morning to dig ditches near the track to divert the water. At the same time, he ordered small workers from each road section to check the track and carry out repairs. Fortunately, there was no mountain soil blockage in this section, making it easier to start work. Therefore, by about 6:00 PM yesterday, almost all the danger had been averted. However, the Zhenjiang section was difficult to restore due to the mountain soil and the mountainous terrain, making it difficult to dig ditches and even more time-consuming to remove the mountain soil from the tracks. Therefore, it is still difficult to restore temporarily, and it will probably take another one or two days to complete the project. As for the losses of the affected residents along the way, they are countless and difficult to estimate at present.

▲ Traffic Conditions Yesterday (25th), the upstream and downstream passenger trains on the railway operated as usual, but only to Zhenjiang South Gate Station. Traffic between Zhenjiang and Nanjing was completely suspended. It is expected that traffic between Zhenjiang and Nanjing can be restored starting today. If there is no heavy rain during the day, the water recedes slightly, and the passage between Zhenjiang and Zhenjiang South Gate Station can also be cleared within one or two days. Today, all trains will still travel between Shanghai and Zhenjiang South Gate Station, it is said. It is still raining in the Zhenjiang area, but the rain in Nanjing has subsided slightly.

▲ Inland River Launches All Stopped

Continuous heavy rain has greatly affected inland river traffic in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. All inland river launches have been completely suspended. The reporter went to the inland river launch bureaus yesterday to conduct an on-site investigation. The known situation is described below:

▲ Lake Routes All Suspended A total of six companies operate morning and evening launch services from Shanghai to Huzhou. When the water rose on the 6th of this month, the morning launch service was suspended, but the night service still operated. Moreover, the Jiahu Line and Xihu Line launches were not blocked. Since the water level receded slightly last week, the morning launch service was also able to resume. However, since the 20th, the heavy rain has continued, and the water level in Huzhou has risen several feet, almost level with the bridge surface. The water police have received an order from the Construction Department to prohibit navigation. As of yesterday, not only were all six morning and evening lines in Shanghai suspended, but also the Jiahu, Suhu, and Xihu boats were completely suspended.

▲ Suzhou Launches All Suspended According to reports from various inland river launch bureaus in this port, the continuous heavy rain has caused the following routes to continue to be suspended: Suxi Line, Suchang Line, Sucheng Line, Zhenqing Line, Kunshan Line, Xipiao Line, Chengxi Line, Yixing, etc., totaling more than 30 routes. Inland river routes have been completely blocked. The reasons for the suspension are as follows: (1) The water is about to reach the level of the rice paddy banks, and villagers do not allow navigation; (2) After the water rises, launches cannot pass under the bridges.

▲ Shanghai Launches Suspended The Suzhou River area is where inland river launches concentrate, including Zhaoshang, Yuantong, Ruishengxiang, Zhengchang, Lixing, Qingji, Yongshun, Yong'an, Yutong, and other launch bureaus, with routes covering the provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. As of yesterday, all of these launches had completely suspended operations. More than 100 launches, company cargo ships, and freighters were docked at the wharves. Because the launches are not operating, the livelihood of the dock workers is also greatly affected.

▲ Zhaoshang Losses The inland river Zhaoshang Bureau has a total of 26 routes. According to an official of the bureau yesterday, 23 routes within Jiangsu Province have been suspended due to flooding. Only the Shensu, Shenhang, and Shenjiao lines can barely operate. Yesterday, the Suzhou launch could not depart, and the Hangzhou launch could still operate if lightly loaded, but not if heavily loaded.

The head office has lost more than 8,000 yuan in the past 20 days due to the impact of the flood, from the 6th of this month to the present. The losses of the branch offices are not included.

▲ Shanghai-Yichang Air Service Temporarily Suspended

The China Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Yichang air service has been temporarily suspended yesterday due to continuous rain, which is not conducive to flying, and the Ming Xiaoling airfield in Nanjing has become a swamp, making it impossible for airplanes to take off and land. It will resume operations depending on the weather.

▲ Telephone Lines in the Concession Blocked

During the torrential rain and thunderstorms yesterday morning, the telephone lines installed by the telephone bureau in the Ningbo Road area of the French Concession suddenly broke down. As a result, telephone users in that area were unable to make calls from yesterday morning until late in the evening. It is reported that the telephone company is now dispatching workers to repair the lines as quickly as possible. It is expected that the situation will be restored to normal today.
