Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Association Seizes a Large Batch of Japanese Goods

▲ Worth About 200,000 Taels

▲ Municipal Chamber of Commerce Starts to Handle Registration

The Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee has been very busy with registration and inspection work in recent days. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, after a resolution passed at the General Meeting of Members, has also begun to register Japanese goods. All member stores belonging to various trade associations can go to collect registration forms. Currently, the customs declaration and transportation industries have resolved not to load or transport Japanese goods due to the strict seizure of goods by the Anti-Japanese Association. The details are recorded as follows:

▲ A Large Batch of Japanese Goods Seized Since the Anti-Japanese Committee announced the measures for the disposal of Japanese goods on the 16th, all Japanese goods are not allowed to be moved. Some unscrupulous merchants took advantage of the inspection work not yet started to rush to load and transport the goods, so that the Japanese inventory was sold out. After hearing the report, the association was very heartbroken, and immediately ordered the inspection section to hurry up and start work in advance. As a result, on the 22nd and 23rd, a large batch of Japanese goods was found at the South Station of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway and the Maigen Road warehouse. The companies and quantities of loading and transportation are as follows: Huatong Company, five boxes of foreign cloth and groceries; Commercial Company, ten boxes and two pieces of groceries, porcelain tableware, galoshes, mast lights, hardware, and straw hats; Dahua Company, two boxes of newspapers; Commercial Company, ten boxes of pigments, mirrors, lampshades, groceries, and galoshes, and one piece of thick cloth; Xueji Yanghe Fine Five Pieces; Gongchang Chong Biji Chong Zhigong Two Boxes; Hengchun Stationery One Box, Smell of Head Medicine, Hardware Yellow Wax Photo Card Seafood Fish Newspaper Groceries Forty-Three Pieces; Shen Tai Transport to Various Places Eleven Boxes; Dong Ji Electric Materials, Felt Hats Four Boxes; Yuantong Transport to Nanjing Four Hundred and Fifty-Two Pieces, Transport to Zhenjiang Sixty-Two Pieces, Transport to Wuxi Two Pieces, Suzhou Six Pieces, Hangzhou Twenty-Nine Pieces; Qingji Piece Goods Cotton Yarn Two Hundred and Seventy-Seven Pieces; Express Piece Goods Package Piece Goods Three Pieces; Hengxing Fine Twill Five Packages, Foreign Cloth Five Disassembled Pieces; Dabing Grade Color Zhigong Ten Boxes. The above-mentioned Japanese goods seized totaled fifty-five boxes, eight hundred and eighty-seven pieces, and five packages. Now, the association believes that this batch of Japanese goods is the first case they have found, and the disposal method cannot but be particularly cautious. It will be submitted to the plenary committee meeting for decision. Before the decision is made, anyone who speaks for the unscrupulous merchants will be severely punished in accordance with the two punitive regulations. It is reported that the total value of these goods is about 250,000 taels. ▲ Chamber of Commerce Handles Registration The Chamber of Commerce began to handle registration yesterday after a resolution passed at the General Meeting of Members. The methods are as follows: (1) The registration of Japanese goods is limited to those purchased before the 14th; (2) During the registration period, all goods must not be moved; (3) After the registration is completed, the goods will be allowed to be sold in accordance with the regulations; (4) The registration is limited to store members belonging to trade associations that have joined the Chamber of Commerce. Non-members should register directly with the Anti-Japanese Association. (6) The registration period ends on August 6th and will not be extended. (6) If the unregistered goods are seized in the future, the Chamber of Commerce will no longer speak on their behalf. (7) Registration forms and all information can be inquired from the Commercial Section.

▲ Customs Declaration Workers Express The Shanghai Customs Declaration Industry Workers' Association sent a letter to the Anti-Japanese Association yesterday, stating that all colleagues in our association, as members of the people, should participate in fulfilling their duties. For this reason, an emergency meeting was convened yesterday to discuss the boycott plan. After the members made various proposals, they thought that the procedures were quite difficult, and the losses from interception and transportation were huge. Therefore, after detailed discussion, it was decided to order all members to clear the procedures in the shortest possible time and stop loading and transporting, so as to be the backing of your association and fulfill the duty of patriotic movement. Therefore, we hereby send a reply in advance, hoping for your consideration.

▲ Bengbu Refuses to Load Japanese Goods The Anti-Japanese Association received a telegram from the Bengbu Transit Association yesterday, sent on the 22nd, which reads: To the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Association, the people across the country are indignant at the massacre of overseas Chinese in the Wanbaoshan case. Today's general meeting of our association unanimously resolved to implement the boycott of Japanese goods from today, based on your association's telegram. In addition to notifying the industry, we will refuse to load and unload from today. Bengbu Transit Association kowtows.

A Letter from the Color Printing Association A letter from the Color Printing Industry Association to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce reads: To the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, we respectfully start. Since the tragic case of the Korean overseas Chinese occurred, all people with blood are indignant. The accumulation of weakness in our country is not enough to make Japan realize that if the people of the whole country do not unanimously implement economic severance. It has been found that the number of colored printed products used in various industries in the city is very large, especially the cigarette industry, which often orders from Japanese-owned printing factories, and the annual leakage is huge. Our association has repeatedly advised various industries that all printed products used by Chinese should be ordered from Chinese printing factories in order to recover the rights and interests. At this time, when the whole country is boycotting Japanese goods, I think the patriotic heart of the cigarette industry and all industries must be sympathetic. The items that have always been ordered from Japanese printing factories must have been automatically changed to Chinese printing factories. However, it is still inevitable that people who are hesitant to wait and see. Please ask your association to notify all industries that all kinds of printed products will be printed by Chinese printing factories in the future, and implement economic severance with Japanese businessmen to wash away national humiliation. I can't hope enough. The Shanghai Color Printing Industry Association starts.

▲ Notice from the Grain and Oil Industry Association The Grain, Oil, and Oilcake Industry Association convened a general meeting of all colleagues yesterday to discuss the Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Affair and the handling of Japanese goods. After public resolution, (A) all kinds of spot goods transported by Japanese ships that have arrived in Shanghai or have been stored in Japanese warehouses, (B) all kinds of road goods that have been transported by Japanese ships but have not yet arrived in Shanghai, (C) all orders for wheat from Europe, America, and Australia, and Xiangmi rice from Yangon and Saigon, etc., that have been ordered from Japanese companies, (D) all goods that have been ordered from Western companies, have been ordered on Japanese ships, but have not yet been transported. The above four items must be truthfully registered with our association from today until July 27. Those who do not comply with the registration deadline will be rejected from buying and selling by our association. The registration method is that all colleagues who transport goods by Japanese ships or store them in Japanese warehouses should copy the

list or detailed account and submit it to our association for registration. After our association receives the list or detailed account, it will stamp the receipt. All our colleagues must comply with the announcement of the resolutions to the industry. This matter is related to foreign affairs, so please do not make a mistake.

▲ Notice from the Transit Industry Association The Shanghai-Hangzhou Transit Industry Association issued a notice yesterday regarding the refusal to transport Japanese goods, which reads: It is for public announcement that the whole country is angry at the tragic abuse of overseas Chinese by the Japanese. Implementing economic severance is the main plan. Now the Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee has been established in the city. Our industry also belongs to the people, and there is no difference. Except for the Japanese goods that have been entrusted to transport earlier and are still stranded in the warehouse due to the lack of vehicles, and have been checked out, and are waiting for a quiet settlement to avoid losing money, after the temporary members' conversation, it was decided to refuse to transport Japanese goods, and to add a penalty to those who change their appearance and secretly entrust the goods, and those who take the risk to transport them. This is hereby announced, hoping for the understanding of all circles.

Yu Qiaqing's Talk on Boycotting Japanese Goods

The National News Agency reporter met with Mr. Yu Qiaqing yesterday and asked if there were any supplements to the speech that Mr. Yu gave at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce General Meeting of Members on the 25th, as reported in today's newspapers. Mr. Yu said that there were still some errors and omissions in the manuscript, so he made the following questions: (Question) Has Mr. Yu attended the Anti-Japanese Association meeting? (Answer) I have not attended. (Question) Why not? (Answer) Because the association elected me as the chairman, and the scope of economic severance is too broad, and the chairman should be any one of the chairman's group of the Chamber of Commerce, because merchants should be the main body of the boycott. (Question) Since Mr. Yu did not attend the Anti-Japanese Association, why did he attend the Chamber of Commerce yesterday? (Answer) Because I am a member of the Chamber of Commerce, and the Chamber of Commerce held a General Meeting of Members yesterday, and it is my duty to attend. And I am afraid that various industries may have various misunderstandings, so I can explain everything. Now I will tell you what I said yesterday again. When this boycott movement occurred, Japanese yarn rose sharply by 20 taels, and domestic yarn also rose by 3 or 4 taels. Merchants from all over the country rushed to buy Japanese goods, and the Japanese goods in Shanghai were transported and loaded empty. These are all done by those who seek profit. As for the economic severance advocated by the Anti-Japanese Association, the scope is very broad, and it is not something that merchants can do. What merchants do is only to rely on their conscience and automatically boycott. Therefore, the boycott can only be done by merchants uniting on their own. As for the methods and abuses, the patriotic boycott movement in our country should follow the boycott methods of the Japanese people. Take a look at the Japanese people living abroad. All daily necessities are used from their own country. It can be seen that the Japanese people's patriotic boycott is all from the conscience and has become a habit. It is not just talking about the boycott on the mouth, but the movement to carry out the story. The boycott should also have a certain scope. For example, raw materials that China does not have and other countries do not have cannot be boycotted, so as not to cause factories to stop and workers to lose their jobs. In this boycott, workers should work harder to manufacture and produce more goods, and do not leave the factory to join the movement, so that they will have strength. Capitalists should also set up more factories, and factories should not take the opportunity to raise prices. On the part of the Chinese people, they must be united and cooperative. For those who operate Japanese goods, they should not be made to suffer unwarranted losses, so that they can gradually switch to selling domestic products. And the existing Japanese goods should be cleared periodically, so as to avoid social and economic losses. I am very opposed to the quick seizure of goods, and the Chamber of Commerce did not notify in advance, and the procedures are too hasty. The Chamber of Commerce should ask the Anti-Japanese Association to return the seized Japanese goods. On the government's side, it is a mistake to increase tariffs on the export of local goods. It should increase import taxes and reduce export taxes, so that domestic goods can be in a protected position. Fortunately, the authorities have realized this, and are in the process of reducing and exempting export taxes on local goods. Moreover, the country is now in a time of trouble. In the north, there is Shi Yusan, in the south, there is the division of Guangdong, and in the middle, there is the rampant of the Communist Party. The government's position is very difficult. Japan takes the opportunity to commit violence. The Chinese people should take care of both internal and external affairs, and act cautiously. Do not indulge in a moment of anger, and leave a pain that will be bitten in the navel. (Question) Does the first person have other insights? (Answer) The Japanese authorities are divided into two factions, one faction is aggressive, and the other is peaceful. Therefore, our people should not treat the Japanese authorities the same. As for the people in their country, as far as I know, most of them advocate friendship with our country. When I went to Japan, there were 20,000 to 30,000 people at the Tokyo National Congress who declared that they did not support their government's aggressive policy and were very willing to be friendly with China. Therefore, our country should pay attention to the actions of the Japanese government. Therefore, this incident is determined to be the purpose of backing up diplomacy. This response should focus not only on the issues of punishing the murderers, apologizing, and compensating, but also on the prompt signing of a fair and equal commercial treaty between China and Japan, so that the relationship between China and Japan has legal protection. Moreover, this point can also prove whether the Japanese government is friendly to China or is an aggressor against China. Because the old Sino-Japanese treaty has been abolished, and the new treaty has not been concluded, it is actually an international country without a treaty. Therefore, whether the Japanese government is willing to conclude a fair and equal treaty with China is a major boundary between its aggression and friendship.

When passing through Baoding, he was questioned and detained by inspectors, mistaken for a member of Shi Yousan's troops. He was detained for a day before being released after a detailed explanation by a friend.' Recently, rumors have resurfaced, and the spread of gossip can easily lead to misinformation and confusion. Although I lack learning and skills, I am filled with righteousness. For as long as I live, I will never do anything ungrateful or disloyal, to be scorned by the group or cursed by posterity. As for Shi's character, please allow me to explain it to you, my superior. Last January, he was forced into a difficult situation in Bengbu and repeatedly sought help. At that time, I was in western Henan and marched urgently through the rain to his aid. Later, when he retreated to Guide, adjacent to our defense zone, we agreed on a mutual defense alliance. However, he retreated to Zhengzhou overnight without notifying us, leaving my troops surrounded. In the battle of Bozhou, my entire army nearly perished. This is the first instance of his lack of trustworthiness. Later, when the main force suffered losses and retreated across the river, his troops confiscated over four thousand of our guns, adding insult to injury by taking advantage of our vulnerability. This is the second instance of his lack of trustworthiness. Such instances are too numerous to list. It speaks poorly of one's judgment to be unaware of such things. Throughout my life, what I have been admired for is trust and righteousness, and what I respect is integrity. What can I gain from Shi? Furthermore, since coming under your command for reorganization, the officers and soldiers have been well-provided for with clothing and food. Stationing in Huanpu has given us a good leader. We obey orders and remain steadfast. However, the newspapers spread rumors, and busybodies refer to 'Shi and Sun' or 'Sun and Shi.' This is truly being overly clever, judging Kuiyuan with the mind of a petty person. Although Kuiyuan is foolish, he would not stoop so low. Past events are vivid in my mind, and there is no need for further explanation. However, I am concerned that rumors may affect my reputation and that the movement of officers and soldiers returning home may be hampered. I earnestly hope that you will consider my sincerity and issue orders to all troops to exempt officers and soldiers of my division returning home with proper registration from inspection. This is my earnest hope. I offer my sincere and direct statement, and I humbly request your consideration. I have entrusted Councilor Fu with a personal report on all matters concerning my troops, and I believe he can provide further details.' Respectfully submitted, Xiong Shihui. [Seal]"

The Third District Party Headquarters Exposes Chen Youren's Conspiracy to Go to Japan

▲Flattering the Japanese Side and Secretly Selling Out the Country

▲The Entire Nation Should Pay Attention

The Third District Party Headquarters of this city issued a circular telegram yesterday, stating: "On the 23rd of this month, Shanghai newspapers reported that Chen Youren and his wife, along with Liu Jiwen and Gan Jihou, dispatched by the Guangdong faction, arrived in Japan this morning (i.e., the 22nd) at 6:40 a.m. aboard the Japanese postal ship 'Kitano Maru' and immediately proceeded to Tokyo. They are scheduled to spend a week discussing Sino-Japanese issues with Japanese Foreign Minister Shidehara and figures from the Japanese government and opposition parties. On the ship, Chen Youren changed his name to the Japanese name 'Toyama Yuzo,' and his wife changed her name to 'Michiko.' After landing, they avoided all meetings. Before Chen's departure for Japan, the Guangdong faction first declared to the Japanese Consul-General in Guangdong, acting on behalf of Suma, that they were specially dispatching Chen Youren and others to exchange views with the Japanese foreign affairs authorities. The Japanese government replied that they could not be received as official representatives but could be treated as prominent figures from a neighboring country, etc. After reading this, doubts arose. The illegitimacy of the pseudo-government in Guangdong has been clearly announced to the people and the world by our National Government. Neither the people of the country nor the various countries of the world recognize it as a legitimate government. Now, Chen Youren and others are going to Japan under the mandate of the Guangdong pseudo-government to discuss Sino-Japanese issues and engage in some secret agreement. Their illegal actions are obvious. The Japanese government, instead of rejecting them as an interference in our country's internal strife, treats them as prominent figures from a neighboring country in an attempt to conceal their intentions. This clearly shows that the Guangdong faction is colluding with Japanese imperialism in an attempt to prolong the life of their reactionary group, and that Japanese imperialism is using the Guangdong reactionary group in an attempt to prolong the internal strife in our country. Otherwise, why would Chen Youren and the others all change into Japanese names and avoid all meetings after landing? Their attempt to ingratiate themselves with Japanese imperialism and engage in a secret agreement and treasonous acts is clear for all to see. Japan has always been unwilling to see the realization of peaceful unification in our country. Whenever there is internal strife and reaction in our country, they will take the opportunity to spread rumors and confuse right and wrong. Although they claim on the surface that inviting Chen Youren and others is not a recognition of the reactionary faction by the Japanese side, their attitude towards the internal strife in our country remains the same. Sino-Japanese issues, as well as the recent tragic incident in Japan and Korea, are naturally handled through negotiations by our legitimate National Government. Since the Guangdong pseudo-government is illegal, what right do they have to preside over these matters? What basis does the Japanese side have to accept negotiations? The Japanese side's invitation to Chen Youren and others is actually a way to delay Sino-Japanese issues, directly and indirectly providing the Guangdong faction with various conveniences, prolonging the internal strife in our country, and allowing them to profit from it. This is very clear. This committee clearly sees their hidden motives and discerns their treachery. In addition to requesting the Central Committee to immediately instruct the general branch in Japan to pay close attention and to forward this to the National Government to immediately notify the Japanese Party authorities to refuse Chen and others' negotiations and to expel them from the country, we are exposing their conspiracy to the world. We hope that all countries in the world will pay attention together. If the Japanese side accepts Chen's negotiations and exchanges views and engages in any secret agreement, they should be unanimously rejected. This is a special telegram. We hope you will take note. The Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special City Third District of the Chinese Kuomintang, bows with seal."

Chen Jilie, Executive Committee Member of the French Branch, Discusses Overseas Chinese's Eager Hope for Peaceful Unification

▲Returning to China to Report to the Central Committee on Party Affairs and the Situation of Overseas Chinese

▲The Education of the Children of Chinese Laborers Who Participated in the War

The French branch of the Chinese Kuomintang has specially dispatched Chen Jilie, a member of the executive committee, as a representative to return to the country to report to the Central Committee on party affairs and the situation of overseas Chinese. Mr. Chen arrived in Shanghai yesterday. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency interviewed him at his residence and had the following conversation: (The mission of this trip) Mr. Chen is a graduate of the Department of Law of Peking University, a Master of Law from the Faculty of Law of the University of Paris, a graduate of the Paris Municipal Academy, and a member of the executive committee of the French branch. This time, he is returning to the country to report to the Central Committee on the situation of the French branch's party affairs, party fees, and the needs of the party affairs address. He will also present the situation of overseas Chinese to express the wishes of the students of the University of Paris. (Overseas Chinese hope for governance) Overseas Chinese hope for peaceful unification in the country and for the increase of our international status. This is extremely urgent. The Guangdong incident was caused by differences in political views and extreme actions. This kind of situation is a necessary phenomenon in politics and is not surprising at first. However, even if political views are different and disputes are fierce, everyone must have a common principle to uphold, that is, no matter what, military force should never be used as the backing of political disputes, opening the door to slaughter and causing internal strife to spread. Moreover, now that the red disaster is rampant and bandits are everywhere, the oppression of aggressive ideologies is increasing. At this time, if we start a conflict and destroy peaceful unification, our international status will plummet, and there will be no day to abolish unequal treaties. Our party governs with party principles and adopts a democratic centralism system for the use of party power and political power. All proposals can be publicly promoted, legally discussed, reconciled with law and justice, and finally decided by the majority. Therefore, not using military force as the backing of political disputes and actually implementing a democratic centralism system is the principle that everyone should jointly abide by to resolve the current situation. (Chinese laborers who participated in the war) During the European War, Chinese laborers who participated in the war helped France a lot. Therefore, there are many Chinese laborers who married in France, and there are quite a few who have children. According to French common practice, even if the children are born of a Chinese father and a French mother, they are still of French nationality. However, they can act freely after the age of twenty-one. Therefore, attention should be paid to the education of these children. If they are not taught Chinese characters and Chinese, will they still have the concept of nationality in the future? The Chinese Laborers Who Participated in the War Committee, organized by the French branch, is currently preparing to establish a Chinese school to provide them with appropriate education. As for the reason for the organization of the committee, it is because French workers are squeezing out Chinese workers, and many Chinese workers have lost their jobs as a result. After repeated negotiations with the French authorities by the committee, many have resumed work, but there are still one or two hundred unemployed. This trip plans to request the Central Committee to find a way to summon them back to the country, give them work to cure the root cause, and allocate funds for relief to treat the symptoms. (Dormitories at the University of Paris) In 1921, the French philanthropist Monsieur Maishu allocated 28 hectares of land to the University of Paris, named it the University City of Paris, and notified various countries that all students studying at the school could build student dormitories in the University City (the site is south of Paris, about five or six Chinese miles) by their respective governments. Many European and American countries have built their own dormitories, but we are the only ones who have not. At that time, there were more than 600 Chinese students in France, who formed a preparatory committee for the Chinese Students Association of the University City of Paris to promote the construction of this building, but so far they have not been able to do so. (Paris newspapers) The Chinese newspaper in Paris, "Party Voice in Europe," promotes the Three Principles of the People. It has now ceased publication. "Zhongshan Daily" promotes news from the motherland and general overseas Chinese. "New China" introduces news from the motherland to the French people in Western languages to make them understand the true situation of our country. (Gao Lu returns to China) Mr. Chen departed from France on May 30. He made short stays in Switzerland, Singapore, and Annam along the way. Before leaving, he met with Minister Gao and learned that he was about to return to China, but there was no definite date at that time. (Entering Beijing soon) Mr. Chen originally planned to enter Beijing today, but the Shanghai-Beijing road was blocked by water, so he will have to wait a little longer. He will enter Beijing as soon as the trains are running.

The Sichuan Fellow Association Cables the National Government to Prohibit Liu Wenhui from Purchasing Foreign Weapons

The Sichuan Fellow Association in Shanghai telegraphed the National Government yesterday, stating: "The province of Sichuan suffers greatly from excessive military presence. To have one province's people supporting three or four hundred thousand troops is truly a unique and strange phenomenon in the country. Supposedly, this is to take on national defense, but we see Xikang, which is as close as lips and teeth, being almost entirely occupied by Tibetan bandits, and we never hear of them increasing troops to go to Kang. Supposedly, this is to transform it into a military industry, but the result of the continuous recruitment of troops by the various armies is that we only see the chemical industry becoming soldiers, and we do not see the transformation of soldiers into workers. The military disasters suffered by the people cannot be described in words. All those who care about Sichuan affairs regard the reorganization and demobilization of troops as the only urgent task at present. However, Liu Wenhui, the chairman of Sichuan Province, and Liu Xiang, the director of post-war affairs, are secretly establishing military factories and purchasing foreign weapons to expand their military power. At the same time, they are requesting the Central Committee to issue post-war public bonds and provincial public bonds, claiming to use them for the reorganization and demobilization of troops. According to a reliable investigation by this association, in addition to Liu Xiang's control of key points along the Yangtze River, allowing him to purchase weapons from foreign countries at any time, the number of guns in his troops has increased from more than 30,000 to more than 100,000 since 1927, and there are also various new types of weapons. Liu Wenhui also sent Xiang Yuren to Shanghai with 11.5 million yuan in cash to purchase weapons from the Jiguo Company. A batch has already been shipped back, but it was seized by Wang Lingji, the commander of Liu Xiang's troops, in Wanxian. Wenhui's trip to Chongqing this time is to negotiate this matter with Liu Xiang. The two Lius requested the issuance of public bonds, claiming that they were unable to reorganize and demobilize troops due to a lack of funds. Judging from the above facts, their so-called use of public bonds to save the poor and save the army is becoming increasingly clumsy, and they have exposed their true colors. This association has a responsibility to save Sichuan, so we earnestly request your government to: (1) Strictly order all troops in Sichuan to stop purchasing weapons from foreign countries, and order the Ministry of Military Affairs not to issue weapons passports indiscriminately to Sichuan military leaders. (2) Order the Ministry of Military Affairs to send personnel to take over the Chengdu and Chongqing armories and other gun factories, and bring them all under state ownership, prohibiting any military personnel from privately owning them. (3) Telegraph Liu Xiang, ordering him to hand over the military equipment seized from Liu Wenhui in Wanxian to the Central Committee and not to use it without authorization. (4) Instruct the customs offices along the Yangtze River to search and seize the military equipment that Liu Wenhui and other Sichuan troops continue to transport and confiscate it. (5) Order Liu Xiang and others to submit a roster of the troops to be reorganized and demobilized, and not to request the issuance of demobilization fees or the issuance of any public bonds until the Central Committee has sent personnel to verify and confirm them. The above five points are the only key to stopping the chaos in Sichuan and saving the people of Sichuan today. We believe that your government, as a revolutionary government, will certainly not tolerate the perverse actions of such people and will comfort the people of Sichuan who are looking forward to it. We send this telegram for your consideration and await your instructions. The Sichuan Fellow Association in Shanghai, bows respectfully."

The U.S. Consulate's Statement After the Verdict in the Qu-Ma Case

▲A Letter to the Municipal Government Expressing Regret

The case of U.S. sailors injuring Qu Shixiang and Ma Ruixiang and shooting Gu Jingen has been adjudicated, the details of which have been recorded in previous reports. It is now known that U.S. Consul General Cunningham sent a letter of apology to the Municipal Government yesterday, expressing his goodwill. The original letter is recorded below: "In response to your letter No. 2846 of June 8, which stated that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce forwarded a letter from the Anhui Fellow Association in Shanghai regarding the injury of Qu Shixiang and Ma Ruixiang by U.S. sailors, this Consul General has the following to request your honorable Mayor's attention. As soon as the fight occurred, the U.S. Marine Corps commander in Shanghai was informed, and the commander immediately ordered a detailed investigation. After the investigation, the sailors who participated in the fight were subjected to a military court. This military court is still in progress. To make all parties aware of this unfortunate event, the military court is known to be proceeding fairly and impartially. Repeated trials are open to the public, and the Anhui Fellow Association in Shanghai has also appointed representatives to attend the court. All those found to be responsible for this unfortunate event will be duly punished. Your honorable Mayor can be assured of this and need not worry. The letter also mentions the case of Gu Jingen. After Gu Jingen was shot, the officials in charge of the Public Concession inspected the body on April 23 of this year. 'The case was listed as Huishan No. 4736.' At that time, it was decided that the U.S. sailor opened fire in self-defense. When the inspection was completed, the prosecutor told the deceased's brother that if he disagreed with the ruling, he could file a lawsuit with the U.S. Court for China. Regarding the occurrence of this type of unfortunate event, there is one more point that this Consul General should request your honorable Mayor's attention. That is, any Chinese person who feels aggrieved by any American can report the detailed circumstances and evidence to Dr. Shi, the prosecutor of the U.S. Court for China. If the evidence appears to show a criminal offense, the U.S. prosecutor will immediately file a lawsuit against the American involved without waiting for the plaintiff to proceed. If there is no evidence of criminal conduct, the Chinese person can still file a civil lawsuit against the American with the U.S. Court for China. According to U.S. practice, the procedures for civil lawsuits are slightly different from those for criminal lawsuits. Civil lawsuits are not initiated by the U.S. prosecutor. The person who claims to be harmed must file a lawsuit with the U.S. Court for China against the person who is believed to have caused the harm. As for filing such lawsuits, the U.S. Court for China is available to all Chinese people and will conduct fair and impartial trials at all times. This point is well known to your honorable Mayor and does not require further confirmation from this Consul General. This Consul General deeply regrets the unfortunate occurrences mentioned in the letter. However, the sensationalist announcements in the local newspapers do not help prove the guilt of the parties involved and harm the long-standing cordial relations between our two governments. If the victims file lawsuits with the appropriate courts to determine whether the defendants are guilty or not, such damage to friendship should be avoided. This Consul General earnestly requests your honorable Mayor to forward the points mentioned in this letter to the relevant Chinese organizations and inform them that this Consul General has made a firm guarantee that any American who commits any criminal act will be prosecuted immediately according to law if evidence is presented to this Consul General or to the U.S. prosecutor. Any Chinese person who suffers harm caused by an American can use the U.S. Court for China, and your honorable Mayor can also be assured that the court will render a fair judgment without any doubt. This is because this office fundamentally desires to maintain the friendship that it has always had with the Chinese government and the Chinese people. The foregoing is acknowledged. It is respectfully replied for your information."

Local News Two

Shanghai's Bitter Rain

▲Low-lying Areas Have Become Lakes

▲The Cotton Harvest is Hopeless

Since the heavy rain began on the 6th of this month, accompanied by thunder and lightning, and the unusually cool weather, it has been two weeks. Floods have occurred in various villages, and the rice fields have been almost completely submerged, causing the people of the country to worry. And now, it is the height of summer (the hottest time of the year), but it is still cool and overcast. Late last night, around midnight, suddenly there were flashes of lightning and continuous thunder. In an instant, in the torrential rain, with two claps of thunder, all the lights in the city went out. The residents who were deep in sleep were all awakened by it. Later, although the raindrops were slightly smaller, the heavy rain continued to fall until morning. Yesterday, the rain did not stop all day, and the Fahrenheit temperature dropped to 64 degrees. Even wearing a jacket felt insufficient. The miserable situation in various places in the rain is summarized below.

▲Zhabei Various Places Have Become Lakes All the roads in Zhabei, such as Qiujiang Road, Yuyingtang Road, both sides of the Hanqiao North Pier, Datong Road Puaifang, and Xinhua Lane at the intersection of Jiaotong Road, have all been inundated, with water depths of about one foot in the houses, because the accumulated water cannot be drained in time. Even the customers buying and selling on both sides of the road and the residents have to use planks, etc. to cross the water. Other open areas such as the large open space east of the Maigen Road Station, the open space near the Sun Temple, in front of the Xijin Association, north of Gonghe Xin Road, and both north and south sides of Pushan Road, have all become lakes. Thousands of Jiangbei straw huts are submerged in water, and people can wash rice and vegetables inside the houses. In the evening, they set up beds on the surface of the water to sleep, so everyone is shouting in pain. What is called the hell on earth is probably no more than this.

▲The Temporary Levee of Zhangjia Weir Zhangjia Weir in the countryside near Xinlonghua in this city was suddenly washed away by rainwater. In an instant, the river water poured into the fields, creating a vast expanse of water. The farmers in the nearby villages also gathered together by beating gongs, rushed to fetch agricultural tools, and built a temporary levee overnight in the rain. They rushed to fill the breach with mud, soil, and stone chips. According to the villagers who came to Shanghai from the area yesterday, if the weather does not clear up, the temporary levee they built may be washed away again by heavy rain. Therefore, this work is done day and night, all in the rain.

▲Cotton in the Wusong Area is Hopeless Wusong has been experiencing heavy rain for days. Low-lying villages in the vicinity have turned into lakes, especially the Pao Tai Wan area, which is the worst. It is a vast expanse of water, and most of the straw huts are submerged in the water. The water level of the small rivers around China Public School continues to rise and increase, making drainage difficult, causing it to pour into the school's playground. All kinds of situations are a spectacle to behold. Generally, farmers say that due to excessive rainfall, although the rice fields are not yet affected, the cotton fields have suffered greatly. If the rain continues to fall, the harvest in the future may be hopeless, so everyone is very worried. Also, farmers in Yangxing and Liuxing townships in Baoshan County rely on cotton cultivation for a living. Yesterday, farmers from the area said that the cotton fields have already suffered a disaster, and there is little hope of recovery.

▲Houses Collapsing Everywhere Yesterday, a flat-roofed house at a certain number in Hongzhang Lane, Chuanshenhe Bridge in the city, collapsed at 5:00 p.m. due to years of disrepair and the soaking of continuous rainy days, which caused the foundation of the wall to loosen. Fortunately, it was in the daytime and no one was injured. Also, vendors at the entrance of Yuyuan and various roads and lanes stopped business and cried out in pain. The loss of general cold drink shops is even greater. The straw huts built by poor Jiangbei people in various places in western Shanghai have been washed down by rain everywhere in recent days. Even those that have not collapsed are full of water, and the sound of crying is miserable. It is also often heard that old houses and thatched houses inhabited by farmers in various villages have been washed down and damaged.

Chen Gongzhe's Case of Seducing a Young Girl

▲Under the Pretext of Discussing Studies

▲Enticing the Girl into a Hotel for a Secret Meeting

▲Huang Jianzhen's Tears Flowed Freely

▲Chen Gongzhe Failed to Appear in Court Yesterday

Chen Gongzhe, the Chief of General Affairs Section of the Ministry of Railways of the National Government, is a native of Zhongshan County, Guangdong Province, and is currently 44 years old. Recently, Huang Jianchi, a native of Panyu County, Guangdong Province, residing at No. 286, Shouchun Lane, Miller Road, Hongkou, representing his father Huang Runyou, engaged lawyer Shi Zhuoren to file a criminal complaint with the Special District Court against Chen for seducing his younger sister Huang Jianzhen, etc. The situation has been reported in newspapers. Yesterday morning, this case was heard in the Second Criminal Court by Judge Ge Zhiqin. The plaintiff, Huang Jianchi, his father, Huang Runyou, and the victim, Huang Jianzhen, all arrived in court on time with their agent, lawyer Shi. The defendant, Chen Gongzhe, did not appear. Chen's mother, Zhao, appointed lawyer Huang Yuping to appear in court and request a postponement. The main points of the indictment and the trial proceedings are excerpted below.

▲Main Points of the Indictment

The original complaint roughly stated: "Seducing a woman under the age of twenty to leave the person with parental rights, continuous rape, and an incidental private prosecution, ordering compensation for losses. My younger sister, Huang Jianzhen, is currently eighteen years old. In the first month of this year's lunar calendar, she met the defendant at the home of a friend, Mai Miaojuan, and they exchanged affectionate words and began to associate with each other. However, my family is not wealthy, and Jianzhen's education was intermittent. At that time, Jianzhen had dropped out of school. The defendant, knowing this, took the opportunity to entice Jianzhen, claiming that he was willing to find a school for her and lend her money. On March 1st of the same year, Jianzhen suffered from a toothache, and the defendant introduced her to Dr. Xu Junmin for treatment. On the 11th, he arranged for Jianzhen to meet him at Dr. Xu's office. The defendant made various advances and on April 12th, the defendant sent a letter, using the excuse of discussing Jianzhen's studies, to deceive her into going to the Nanjing Central Hotel, where she was raped four times in a row. He also said that his household lacked a hostess and that he wanted to marry her. Later, Jianzhen learned that the defendant was already married and realized she had been deceived. When she argued with him, he ignored her. When my mother learned of this, she was so angry that she committed suicide by hanging herself. By such actions, the defendant has violated Article 257, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. Therefore, we file this lawsuit and demand that the defendant pay Jianzhen 10,000 yuan for maintenance and 10,000 yuan for consolation."

▲Trial Proceedings

At 10:15 yesterday morning, after Judge Ge took the bench, the defendant's agent, lawyer Huang Yuping, first stated that the defendant had gone to Nanyang two months ago due to business and would not be able to return to the country for several months. He requested a postponement of the trial. Regarding the legal and factual aspects of this case, he reserved all his rights to defend. Then, the plaintiff's lawyer, Shi Zhuoren, stated that when his lawyer wrote to the defendant last time, the defendant was still in Shanghai. Now, he is intentionally absent. He did not object to the defendant's lawyer's request for a postponement, but requested that the date be changed to seven days later to clarify whether the defendant was in Shanghai. He also submitted all the evidence and letters. Huang Jianchi also stated that he worked at the wheel office of the Toyo Trading Company Wharf. Jianzhen is my younger sister, and my father's name is Huang Runyou. He is now old, so I am filing the lawsuit on his behalf. Huang Runyou testified that he was 67 years old and unable to answer the judge's questions because he was from Guangdong and did not understand the Shanghai dialect, and he was hard of hearing. His face was covered with a white beard, so he could not understand what he heard. Then, Huang Jianzhen was called into the witness box. Jianzhen was wearing a gray cloth cheongsam, white socks, and leather shoes, her eyebrows furrowed in sadness, and tears streaming down her face. She looked very pitiful. Judge Ge asked her age, and she replied, "Eighteen." He asked, "Are you studying?" She replied, "I am not studying now." He asked, "Did Chen Gongzhe send you the letter?" She replied, "Yes." He asked, "When did you meet Chen?" She replied, "I met him at Mai's house in the first month." He asked, "On what day did you go to Nanjing and have physical relations?" She replied, "April 14th, at the Central Hotel." At this point, Judge Ge announced that the case would be postponed to August 1st and the defendant would be summoned to court for further verification. He also instructed the plaintiff to bring an interpreter familiar with the Shanghai dialect to the next court hearing to avoid language barriers, as the plaintiff was not proficient in the Shanghai dialect. After the announcement, the court adjourned.

Further Hearing on the Case of Purchasing Military Firearm While Posing as a National Government Military Officer

▲Bick Secretly Reported to Customs

▲Court Investigating Based on This Point

The Russian, Bick, and Leviasky, for forging the seal of Lai Fa Foreign Firm, and impersonating National Government military officers to order military firearm, were detained by the police and brought to the Special District Court. Several hearings have been held, details of which have been published in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Court President Xu Jiayi and Prosecutor Qian Hongye took the bench at the First Criminal Court for further questioning. The police were still represented by lawyer Ru Baoyi. The court appointed interpreter Jiang Baoliang to translate. Court President Xu first questioned Leviasky, who stated that he had previously commissioned Mei Tai Printing House to print cards. One morning, he went to pick them up and met Lai Fa on the way. Lai Fa asked why he had taken the contract and urged him to return it. Because it was inconvenient to argue on the road, he agreed to return it the next day. Lai Fa then asked him to pick up the cards, so he went to Mei Tai, but the owner, He Zixiang, was not there, so he did not get them. However, he saw a hundred copies of the contract that Lai Fa had asked the printing house to print. Seeing that it was related to military firearm, he copied one copy. At 4:00 in the afternoon, he went again, and He Zixiang told him that the cards had been sent to Lai Fa and gave him a copy of the contract, asking him to take it to Lai Fa. He then tore up the copy he had made. Unexpectedly, he was arrested at that time. Moreover, Mei Tai was an old customer of Lai Fa. If he wanted to forge Lai Fa's seal, he would not have asked Mei Tai to make it. Court President Xu then asked He Zixiang about Leviasky's commission to print cards, and then questioned Leviasky, "Did Lai Fa send a letter to Zhang Faying?" He replied, "On the 9th, Lai Fa sent it to Zhang Faying." He asked, "Does the letter say that if you fulfill all the conditions, you will ask Zhu Ziyao and two others to be witnesses?" He replied, "Not Zhang Faying. At that time, because Lai Fa only had one witness, Carlo, and no guarantor, he was angry and refused to sign the contract. Lai Fa then asked Zhu Ziyao to be the guarantor and promised to give him 200 yuan. He then added the word 'guarantor' before the witnesses on the contract, and the names were also added at the same time." The court then summoned Zhu Ziyao, but Zhu did not arrive. He then questioned Lai Fa, "Is what Leviasky said correct?" He replied, "The content of the letter said that if the Nanjing government could approve this matter, he would find two people to be guarantors. But in my opinion, why didn't Zhang Faying submit this letter, but the defendant did? This shows that Zhang never received this letter, so the seal on the contract must have been forged by the defendant." Court President Xu verified the testimony and then declared that the court had inquired with the Jianghai Customs Supervision Office whether Bick had reported Lai Fa's sale of military firearm to Guangdong, but had not yet received a reply. He has now sent a letter urging them to reply. Once the reply arrives, the court will set a date for further questioning. This case will be heard and verified again.

Local Court Destroys Narcotics

The Shanghai Local Court presented a report to the Jiangsu High Court regarding the destruction of the narcotics confiscated in the first half of the 20th year of the Republic, and it was decided to be held on the morning of July 25th. Yesterday was the scheduled date. Representatives from various organizations came to supervise, including Yu Zongjian from the High Court, Xiong Huihua and Chen Jingzhai from the Ministry of Judicial Administration, Huang Chang from the Municipal Government, Lin Woping from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Ju Zhijing from the Special District Local Court, Lu Youchang from the Customs, Chen Jiannan from the Shanghai County Party Department, Fan Ander from the Anti-Drug Association, and the Second District General Office, which sent patrol officer Niu Yulin and several police officers to the site to protect the area. Chief Prosecutor Liu sent Prosecutor Zhao Zikui and a clerk to verify and explain each item. At around 10:00, they ordered police chief Xu Jinqing, police sergeants Chen Xihui and Chen Junfang, etc., to supervise the police to pile the narcotics on the open ground, using pine wood, kerosene, and salt to burn them. Because of the heavy rain yesterday, it took until 2:00 in the afternoon to complete the destruction. The ashes were then packed in sacks and ordered to be sunk to the bottom of the Huangpu River to eliminate the toxic fumes. A total of 5,656 items of narcotics were destroyed this time, including opium, morphine, red pills, and smoking paraphernalia, etc., including more than ten sacks of two wooden boxes.

16,000 Yuan Robbed from the General Trading Trust Company

▲Five Robbers Robbed with Four Guns

▲Police Arrived, but the Robbers Had Already Fled

The General Trading Trust Company at No. 521, Yuxing Lane, Fujian Road, was invaded by five robbers around 8:30 last night. Four of them were armed with guns. At this time, the staff had already rested and gone out, so there were not many people in the office. After the robbers entered the room, they opened boxes and drawers and searched frantically for a long time. Finally, they seized 16,000 yuan in cash and fled. The police were notified and sent officers to investigate, but the robbers had already fled. The General Trading Trust Company also operates a banking business. Yuxing Lane, where it is located, connects to Nanjing Road in the north and Daxin Street in the west, so the robbers could easily change their route. The Old Gate Police Station has already started investigating this case. Most of the stolen banknotes were from the Central Bank.

Municipal Finance Bureau Stops Issuing Merchant Ship Licenses

▲Exemption from Registration Fees for Small Boats

The Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau issued a notice yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of issuing a notice, this bureau, based on the precedents of the former Shanghai Municipal Office, issued merchant ship licenses and ordered small boats to register, charging fees separately, originally for the convenience of customs inspection and release. Now that the Jianghai Customs has been abolished, all types of ships are inspected and registered by this city, numbered, and pay monthly dues. It is hereby announced that merchant ship licenses will be discontinued and fees for small boat registration will be waived from August 1st of this year to show consideration. In addition to reporting to the Municipal Government and ordering the Dongjiadu Ship Dues Office of this bureau to comply, this notice is hereby issued for the information of all boat owners. A special announcement."

General Meeting of the China Photographic Society

▲Passed Amended Constitution

▲Welcome New Members

The China Photographic Society, a photographic academic research group organized by famous domestic photographers, held a general meeting of all members at the Minghua Bank yesterday. Those present included Zhang Zhenhou, Qian Jinghua, Wang Dafo, Ding Song, Lang Jingshan, Zhu Shouren, Guo Xiqi, Shao Woyun, Hu Bozhou, Mo Tianxiang, Cai Renbao, Zhang Liyun, Zhang Zhongshan, Zhou Jianqiao, etc. Mr. Hu Boxiang was elected chairman. First, the new members Tong Boju and Lin Jinlun were welcomed into the society. Mr. Tong is an accountant, a former university professor, and currently the assistant manager of Minghua Bank. Mr. Lin is proficient in law and currently engaged in commerce. Both gentlemen are extremely knowledgeable in photographic academics and have repeatedly exhibited their works at the China Photographic Society exhibition. Next, Wang Dafo, a member of the Constitution Revision Committee, presented the revised constitution, which was discussed item by item and passed by all. The content divides the qualifications of members into three categories, elects nine directors and several committee members to be fully responsible for academic research, and organizes into six major departments: fine arts, technology, color, film, speech, and travel. This constitution was revised with reference to the precedents of photographic associations in various countries and will be published soon for the reference of those who study photography.

Important Proposals of the Leprosy Association

The Chinese Leprosy Relief Association held a board meeting yesterday afternoon at 5:00 at the Maritime Youth Association. Those present included Li Yuanxin, Li Guansen, Ou Weiguo, Wang Zhiren, Cheng Lian, Zhu Shaoping, Yan Fuqing, Wu Jingyao, Wu Zhijian, Mrs. Xiao Zhiji, Mrs. Zheng Yangxiu, etc. The following major proposals were resolved: (1) It was decided to hold the fifth annual meeting at 4:30 pm on July 30th in the Zhongshan Hall of the Youth Association at No. 20, Museum Road. Leprosy expert Dr. Hayshinder will be invited to give a lecture on "The History of Leprosy." (2) It was decided to hold a national leprosy conference in April of the 21st year of the Republic to attract the attention of the Chinese people and discuss concrete plans to eradicate leprosy in China. (3) The number of leprosy patients seeking treatment in the Shanghai First District is increasing day by day. The existing Hongkou Skin Disease Hospital is no longer sufficient. It was decided to raise 50,000 yuan between November and December of this year to build a large-scale clinic in Shanghai for relief.

Unclaimed Opium at the North Railway Station

Recently, the opium ban in the inland areas has been extremely strict. General opium dealers often put opium in wooden boxes, disguised as other goods, and transported them to the inland areas for sale. Yesterday, a large wooden box was found in the baggage room of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway North Railway Station. After inspection by military police, the box was opened, and it was full of opium and red pills and other prohibited items. The packages were marked with the words "Hu receive Zhang receive" and other words. The opium dealers took the opportunity to escape. The opium and other items were immediately seized, weighing more than 300 catties, a total of more than 5,000 taels. After searching for the person transporting the opium without success, the prohibited items were sent to the local court for confiscation and destruction.

Woman Sues for Divorce and Demands 26 Years of Alimony

▲Totaling 28,080 Yuan

A woman, Zhang Sun, recently engaged two lawyers, Wu Chengyu and others, to file a complaint with the Special District Court, accusing her husband, Zhang Zhixiang (of Juntaibao Customs Brokerage, Gongshun Lane, Guangdong Road), of abuse, neglect of maintenance, and forcing her to sign a separation agreement. She requested that a divorce be granted and that she be paid alimony for 26 years, at 90 yuan per month, totaling 28,080 yuan. Furthermore, due to extreme poverty, she was unable to pay the litigation fees and requested assistance in litigation in accordance with Article 130 of the Civil Procedure Law. Yesterday morning, Judge Xu Wenyong of the Special Court opened the Seventh Civil Court for questioning. The defendant engaged lawyer Gu Ren to defend him. Judge Xu first asked the plaintiff's agent, lawyer Wu, why the plaintiff had not paid the litigation fees. Lawyer Wu replied that the divorce should be resolved first in accordance with the law, and then the litigation fees should be paid. Judge Xu said, "How can the proceedings proceed if the litigation fees are not paid? Furthermore, the plaintiff's address is unknown, and the court cannot investigate the plaintiff's economic situation." Lawyer Wu replied that Sun had no ability to pay the litigation fees after being expelled. She is currently living with her sister in the French Concession. Then, the defendant's agent, lawyer Gu Ren, stated that the plaintiff in this case was the defendant's concubine, not his legal wife. They had been cohabiting for ten years and had one child each, a son, Huchen, nine years old, and a daughter, Peilan, three years old. He heard that on the fourth day of the lunar month, the plaintiff was having an affair with a man named Xu in the room while the defendant was away. Because it had been going on for a long time, Zhang broke in and caught the two lovers. Zhang then called the police and arrested the pair, intending to send them to the authorities for investigation. After she begged bitterly, she agreed to separate unconditionally. Zhang also agreed because the family scandal should not be publicized. The next day, his lawyer drafted a separation agreement, which she sealed with her fingerprint. At that time, the defendant gave her 225 yuan in cash and clothing worth 2,000 yuan. Now, she suddenly makes this fuss, which is obviously unreasonable. Moreover, the plaintiff has already received the aforementioned property and hired two lawyers. How can she say that she is unable to pay the litigation fees? It is contrary to both law and reason. He requested that the court reject the plaintiff's complaint. However, Zhang Sun and her lawyer both denied receiving the defendant's property. Judge Xu then announced that the case would be verified again after a written ruling on the request for assistance was made.

Jiangbei Bandit Suppression Command Transfers Bandit Leader Dong Zhengren

Dong Zhengren, a famous bandit leader in Zhenjiang (nickname "Shouer Laba"), was arrested by detective Liu Longdai of the New Gate Police Station for extorting a large sum of money from his fellow villager Zhang Zhenglu. After the police chief found out that Dong was a major bandit in the inland areas, he ordered him to be detained pending investigation. Now, the Pacification Superintendent's Office has learned of this and immediately sent Deputy Commander Chen to Shanghai by car overnight with a document, requesting the police station to extradite him. The police chief agreed to send the major bandit to the court that day. Deputy Commander Chen will go to the court at the appointed time to apply for the transfer to his case.

Tang Yulu's Funeral Held Yesterday

▲Burial Postponed Due to Rain

▲Mrs. Tang Cried Bitterly

The funeral of Mr. Tang Yulu, Confidential Secretary of the Ministry of Finance, who died from injuries, was held at 3:00 pm yesterday at the Universal Funeral Home on Jiaozhou Road. Those who came to pay their respects included Wu Zhihui, a member of the Central Committee, Qian Xinzhi, the envoy to France, Wu Jingxiong, Liu Ruiheng, Yang Xingfo, Guo Biao, Yan Fuqing, Tang Liu, Guo Dehua, and other advisors from the Public Works Department, totaling more than 200 people. Minister of Finance Song Ziwen also sent a representative to pay his respects. Foreign guests included Japanese envoy Shigomitsu

Mrs. Tang Weeping Behind Her Hands (Photo by this Newspaper)

Aoi, and the US Consul General, totaling more than 40 people. The order of the ceremony was: (1) Stand at attention, (2) Pastor Fei Hesheng's worship, (3) Yang Xingfo's report on the incident, (4) Wu Zhihui's speech, (5) Paying respects, (6) Paying respects to the remains, (7) Encoffining, (8) Pastor Fei Hesheng's prayer, (9) The bereaved family thanked the guests. Mrs. Tang arrived at the funeral home by car around 3:00 pm, dressed entirely in black, with a black veil over her head. After entering the door, she covered her face and wept bitterly. When she saw the remains, she cried out loudly, which was extremely tragic. All the Chinese and Western female guests in the hall were moved to tears. The coffin was placed in the main hall, and large and small wreaths were almost completely displayed. After the ceremony, due to the rain, the family members decided to temporarily place the coffin in the funeral home and move it to the Public Works Department Cemetery in Hongqiao for burial at a later date.

Young Woman's Lawsuit Against Husband for Abandonment Dismissed

Xu Qiuyue, a young woman, previously engaged lawyers Dong Yu and Chen Zhigao to file a criminal complaint in the French Court against Chen Jiongwen for abandonment, requesting the recovery of 120,000 yuan in living expenses. After the summons, the defendant did not appear. She was instructed to be summoned again for investigation, as reported in the newspapers. She was summoned again yesterday and first told the lawyers representing the plaintiff that the plaintiff married the defendant as a concubine in 1924. Not long after entering the family, the defendant's wife died. In 1927, the defendant remarried a Zhu as his successor. Unexpectedly, Zhu was naturally fierce and quarrelsome with the plaintiff. The defendant told the plaintiff that it was inevitable that wives and concubines would quarrel, so it would be better to come to Shanghai to rent a house to live in separately. At that time, the plaintiff believed him and came to Shanghai with him. Later, the defendant claimed that it was difficult to find a suitable house for the time being and temporarily lived in a hotel. Unexpectedly, the defendant returned to his hometown alone and never returned, moving away without a trace, abandoning the plaintiff. Now, it was only discovered that the defendant had a foreign goods store under his jurisdiction, so she filed a lawsuit requesting the recovery of living expenses, etc. The defendant, Chen Jiongwen, also defended through a lawyer, stating that the plaintiff's lawyer had omitted an important point. The plaintiff filed a report in your court in 1928, which was then mediated by lawyer Wang Chengji. The defendant paid the plaintiff 1,500 yuan as a settlement. There is a settlement agreement as proof. Since this case has already been settled, how can it be brought again? My client originally wanted to file a counterclaim, but considering that the plaintiff is a woman, he requests that she be severely reprimanded. The plaintiff acknowledged receiving 1,500 yuan, but hesitated about the rest. Judge Zhu reviewed the words and ruled in court that the plaintiff's accusation was untrue. Since this case has already been settled, how can it be brought again? The case should be dismissed immediately.

County Finance Bureau Issues Notice to Collect Busy Silver

The Shanghai County Finance Bureau issued a notice yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of issuing a notice to collect busy silver, according to the case, the upper and lower busy silver in this county have been changed to combined collection since the 18th year of the Republic, which has been reported to the Finance Department for approval. It is now scheduled to start collecting the upper and lower busy silver for the 20th year of the Republic on August 1st, limited to within two months. After two months, an additional 10% will be levied on the regular tax. Calculated, each mu of upper-class arable land shall complete the busy silver for 1 coin, 1 fen, 4 li, 3 hao, 2 si, 7 hu (8 mu, 7 fen, 4 li, 7 hao, combined to complete 1 tael of busy silver), and each mu of allowed arable land shall complete the busy silver for 1 coin, 1 fen, 5 li, 9 hao, 7 si, 9 hu (8 mu, 6 fen, 2 li, 3 hao, combined to complete 1 tael of busy silver). Each tael is converted into 2 yuan and 5 fen in regular and supplementary taxes, with a commission

Page 16

fee of 1 jiao, 2 fen, 3 li.) In addition to the easy-to-understand forms, which are distributed to the 保 by order of the officials, this notice is hereby issued for the information of all the householders in the county. Each of you shall submit the amount to be paid to the counter as scheduled, draw a serial number, and settle the account, and be careful not to wait and delay, so as not to incur investigation. This notice is of utmost importance."

Workers in Public Utilities May Not Stop Work on Any Holiday

▲Joint Notice from the Municipal Public Utilities and Social Affairs Bureaus

The Municipal Public Utilities and Social Affairs Bureaus issued a joint notice yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of issuing a joint notice, Article 19 of the Factory Law promulgated by the National Government on December 30th, 1929, states that 'Regarding the work of military and public utilities, the competent authorities may, when deemed necessary, stop the workers' holidays,' etc. Indeed, public utilities, including water, electricity, and transportation, are all related to the lives of the people and cannot be lacking for even a moment. Moreover, they are all related to local security and cannot be interrupted for even a moment. The government has the responsibility to protect the people and maintain local order, so it is necessary to stop the holidays of workers in public utilities factories. Although the law will not be implemented until August 1st of this year, Shanghai is a huge city in China with 3 million citizens, and the importance of public utilities is unmatched by other places. Historically, various holidays in the industrial and commercial sectors, in addition to certain mass movements or certain commemorative ceremonies, workers in municipal public utilities factories have mostly not participated in their entirety, and the people and the locality have been able to be safely protected. Therefore, this bureau and others, based on Article 19 of the Factory Law, jointly announce that all workers in various public utilities companies in the city will only be allowed to send representatives to participate in any mass movements or commemorative ceremonies in the future, and all other workers must continue to work as usual. Even on other holidays, they may not stop work. It is hoped that all workers in the public utilities companies will comply. This is announced."

Zhu Qinglan Goes from Shaanxi to Gansu to Survey Disaster

▲ Shaanxi Relief Completed

▲ Continuing to Gansu to Investigate the Disaster

Zhu Ziqiao, Standing Committee Member of the Relief Commission and Chairman of the North China Charitable Federation, came to Shanghai twice previously to organize a temporary emergency relief association for the Shaanxi disaster with representatives from various countries and philanthropists. He raised over 431,000 yuan in donations, which were successively remitted to Shaanxi. He also took relief workers to various counties in Shaanxi to distribute aid. The disaster victims all benefited practically and sang his praises. Now, because the Shaanxi relief is completed, Mr. Zhu is transferring to Gansu to investigate the disaster situation. The disaster in Gansu is severe, no less than in Shaanxi, but because it is located on the frontier, and transportation is far and difficult, there is suffering from the inability to provide relief. Even with relief funds, it is not easy to distribute them. Mr. Zhu, undeterred by hardship, resolutely went to provide aid. He telegraphed Chairman Ping Jingren of the Relief Commission and Mr. Wang Yiting, requesting them to raise funds to investigate and relieve the Gansu disaster, in order to save the people of Longxi who are on the verge of death. He telegraphed again the day before yesterday, reporting that he had departed from Shaanxi for Gansu on the 22nd of this month. The two telegrams are recorded below: (1) To Chairman Xu, Elder Wang, and forwarded to Huang Hanzhi, Zhang Xianqing, Li Shoushan, Wu Zhihao, Li Zuzui, and all philanthropists: Because the disaster in Gansu is severe, I wanted to go and inspect. Yesterday, someone from eastern Long came and said that in the Zhenyuan area, there was no harvest of wheat, and there was also banditry. Hearing this, I felt saddened. The disaster in Longxi is even more severe. I plan to go there in person soon. Gentlemen, please practice the Bodhisattva path and raise generous relief funds to save the dying people of Gansu and Longxi. I earnestly pray. Zhu Qinglan, 30th. (2) To Chairman Xu of the Relief Commission, Elder Wang, and forwarded to Huang Hanzhi, Zhang Xianqing, Wu Zhihao, Li Zuzui, and all gentlemen, as well as all philanthropists: Yang Chen and I, along with relief colleagues, are going to Gansu to inspect the disaster situation. More details will follow. Zhu Qinglan.

Continued Report on the Disaster Situation in Jiangxi

The Shanghai fundraising for Jiangxi emergency relief association has previously received telegrams from disaster investigators Wei Ruifeng, Wu Jiasan, and Ma Geng, reporting on everything. Now we have received a report as follows: (Above omitted) Keqiang and others were dispatched to Jiangxi and observed on the ship that along the Yangtze River, it was a vast expanse of water. Fields and houses were submerged in the water, and the disaster was already formed. When they arrived in Jiujiang, the city was flooded by the river, and the streets and alleys were filled with water, forming a waterlogged area. They immediately went to the Jiujiang Red Cross Branch to investigate the disaster situation, and met with Chairman Zhan Mingqiu, President Zhang Fengqi, and the hospital director of the Song Hospital. They discussed that the Jiangxi disaster was different from other provinces because Jiangxi Province was suffering from banditry, so the damage was more severe and relief was more difficult. For example, the Jingdezhen porcelain industry has no capital and all the laid-off workers are unemployed, and there is an urgent need to find ways to raise funds to establish a lending institution to provide relief. This is one aspect of the disaster situation investigated in Jiujiang. After arriving in Nanchang, they met Commander Xiong. Commander Xiong also knew very well that the gentlemen in Shanghai urgently wanted to understand the real situation of the Jiangxi disaster, so he immediately gave instructions and asked Keqiang to telegraph first to comfort the expectations of the great philanthropists in Shanghai. Now Nanchang has organized a local relief office, which is directly under the office of the Director of the Party and Government Committee of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, Wen Qun. All Jiangxi disaster affairs are handled by this office. Keqiang and others are now assisting in the handling of affairs everywhere. The office has received telegrams from various places requesting relief and is in urgent need of finding ways to provide relief. A list of refugees requesting relief is enclosed, which shows the severity of the disaster situation in various places in the province, and so on. Now the association has already telegraphed 200,000 yuan for relief to Commander Xiong in Nanchang to handle at his discretion. (List of refugees requesting relief omitted)

Mild Cholera Discovered in the City

▲ Investigation by the Municipal Health Bureau

Continuous moldy rain, inconsistent cold and warm weather, and carelessness at night often lead to catching colds. According to the investigation by the Municipal Health Bureau in the past week, there are many patients with gastrointestinal diseases in various hospitals. Similar symptoms of cholera have been found in various hospitals. According to the investigation by the bureau's personnel, the feces of those suffering from similar cholera diseases were tested and confirmed to be non-virulent cholera, which is not life-threatening. However, at the beginning of the cholera outbreak, citizens should be cautious about hygiene, eat less raw and cold food and unclean melons and fruits, be careful about their daily life, and moderate their diet, and then they can be immune to severe infection.
